# <a name="routing-in-aspnet-core"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-103">Roteamento no ASP.NET Core</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-103">Routing in ASP.NET Core</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-104">Por [Ryan Nowak,](https://github.com/rynowak) [Kirk Larkin](https://twitter.com/serpent5)e [Rick Anderson](https://twitter.com/RickAndMSFT)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-104">By [Ryan Nowak](https://github.com/rynowak), [Kirk Larkin](https://twitter.com/serpent5), and [Rick Anderson](https://twitter.com/RickAndMSFT)</span></span>

::: moniker range=">= aspnetcore-3.0"

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-105">O roteamento é responsável por corresponder às solicitações HTTP recebidas e despachar essas solicitações para os pontos finais executáveis do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-105">Routing is responsible for matching incoming HTTP requests and dispatching those requests to the app's executable endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-106">[Os pontos finais](#endpoint) são as unidades do aplicativo de código executável de tratamento de solicitações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-106">[Endpoints](#endpoint) are the app's units of executable request-handling code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-107">Os pontos finais são definidos no aplicativo e configurados quando o aplicativo é iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-107">Endpoints are defined in the app and configured when the app starts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-108">O processo de correspondência de ponto final pode extrair valores da URL da solicitação e fornecer esses valores para o processamento de solicitações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-108">The endpoint matching process can extract values from the request's URL and provide those values for request processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-109">Usando informações de ponto final do aplicativo, o roteamento também é capaz de gerar URLs que mapeiam para pontos finais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-109">Using endpoint information from the app, routing is also able to generate URLs that map to endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-110">Os aplicativos podem configurar o roteamento usando:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-110">Apps can configure routing using:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="444c2-111">Controladores</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-111">Controllers</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="444c2-112">Páginas do Razor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-112">Razor Pages</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="444c2-113">SignalR</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-113">SignalR</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="444c2-114">serviços gRPC</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-114">gRPC Services</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="444c2-115">Middleware habilitado [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) para endpoint, como [verificações de saúde](xref:host-and-deploy/health-checks).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-115">Endpoint-enabled [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) such as [Health Checks](xref:host-and-deploy/health-checks).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="444c2-116">Delegados e lambdas registrados com roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-116">Delegates and lambdas registered with routing.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-117">Este documento abrange detalhes de baixo nível do roteamento ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-117">This document covers low-level details of ASP.NET Core routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-118">Para obter informações sobre a configuração do roteamento:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-118">For information on configuring routing:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-119">Para os controladores, veja <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-119">For controllers, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-120">Para convenções de <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>Páginas de Barbear, veja .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-120">For Razor Pages conventions, see <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-121">O sistema de roteamento de ponto final descrito neste documento se aplica a ASP.NET Núcleo 3.0 e posterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-121">The endpoint routing system described in this document applies to ASP.NET Core 3.0 and later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-122">Para obter informações sobre o <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>sistema de roteamento anterior baseado em , selecione a versão ASP.NET Core 2.1 usando uma das seguintes abordagens:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-122">For information on the previous routing system based on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>, select the ASP.NET Core 2.1 version using one of the following approaches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-123">O seletor de versão para uma versão anterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-123">The version selector for a previous version.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-124">Selecione [ASP.NET roteamento Core 2.1](https://docs.microsoft.com/aspnet/core/fundamentals/routing?view=aspnetcore-2.1).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-124">Select [ASP.NET Core 2.1 routing](https://docs.microsoft.com/aspnet/core/fundamentals/routing?view=aspnetcore-2.1).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-125">[Exibir ou baixar código de exemplo](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples/3.x) ([como baixar](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-125">[View or download sample code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples/3.x) ([how to download](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span></span>

## <a name="routing-basics"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-128">Conceitos básicos sobre roteamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-128">Routing basics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-129">Todos os modelos ASP.NET Core incluem roteamento no código gerado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-129">All ASP.NET Core templates include routing in the generated code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-130">O roteamento é registrado no `Startup.Configure`pipeline [de middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) em .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-130">Routing is registered in the [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) pipeline in `Startup.Configure`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-131">O código a seguir mostra um exemplo básico de roteamento:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-131">The following code shows a basic example of routing:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet&highlight=8,10)]

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-132">O roteamento usa um par <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseRouting*> de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>middleware, registrados por e:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-132">Routing uses a pair of middleware, registered by <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseRouting*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-133">`UseRouting`adiciona correspondência de rota ao pipeline de middleware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-133">`UseRouting` adds route matching to the middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-134">Este middleware analisa o conjunto de pontos finais definidos no aplicativo e seleciona a [melhor correspondência](#urlm) com base na solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-134">This middleware looks at the set of endpoints defined in the app, and selects the [best match](#urlm) based on the request.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-135">`UseEndpoints`adiciona execução de ponto final ao pipeline de middleware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-135">`UseEndpoints` adds endpoint execution to the middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-136">Ele executa o delegado associado ao ponto final selecionado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-136">It runs the delegate associated with the selected endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-137">O exemplo anterior inclui uma única *rota para* o ponto final de código usando o método [MapGet:](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-137">The preceding example includes a single *route to code* endpoint using the [MapGet](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*) method:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-138">Quando uma `GET` solicitação HTTP é `/`enviada para a URL raiz:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-138">When an HTTP `GET` request is sent to the root URL `/`:</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-139">O delegado de solicitação mostrado executa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-139">The request delegate shown executes.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-140">`Hello World!`é escrito para a resposta HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-140">`Hello World!` is written to the HTTP response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-141">Por padrão, a `/` `https://localhost:5001/`URL raiz é .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-141">By default, the root URL `/` is `https://localhost:5001/`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-142">Se o método `GET` de solicitação não `/`for ou a URL raiz não for, nenhuma rota corresponde e um HTTP 404 será devolvido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-142">If the request method is not `GET` or the root URL is not `/`, no route matches and an HTTP 404 is returned.</span></span>

### <a name="endpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-143">Ponto de extremidade</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-143">Endpoint</span></span>

<a name="endpoint"></a>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-144">O `MapGet` método é usado para definir um **ponto final**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-144">The `MapGet` method is used to define an **endpoint**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-145">Um ponto final é algo que pode ser:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-145">An endpoint is something that can be:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-146">Selecionado, combinando o método URL e HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-146">Selected, by matching the URL and HTTP method.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-147">Executado, executando o delegado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-147">Executed, by running the delegate.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-148">Os pontos finais que podem ser combinados e `UseEndpoints`executados pelo aplicativo são configurados em .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-148">Endpoints that can be matched and executed by the app are configured in `UseEndpoints`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-149">Por <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>exemplo, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*> [métodos semelhantes](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions) conectam os delegados de solicitação ao sistema de roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-149">For example, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>, and [similar methods](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions) connect request delegates to the routing system.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="444c2-150">Métodos adicionais podem ser usados para conectar ASP.NET recursos da estrutura Core ao sistema de roteamento:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-150">Additional methods can be used to connect ASP.NET Core framework features to the routing system:</span></span>
- [<span data-ttu-id="444c2-151">MapRazorPages para Páginas de Navalha</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-151">MapRazorPages for Razor Pages</span></span>](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RazorPagesEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRazorPages*)
- [<span data-ttu-id="444c2-152">Controladores de mapas para controladores</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-152">MapControllers for controllers</span></span>](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllers*)
- [<span data-ttu-id="444c2-153">MapHub\<THub> para SignalR</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-153">MapHub\<THub> for SignalR</span></span>](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.SignalR.HubRouteBuilder.MapHub*) 
- [<span data-ttu-id="444c2-154">MapGrpcService\<TService> para gRPC</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-154">MapGrpcService\<TService> for gRPC</span></span>](xref:grpc/aspnetcore)

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-155">O exemplo a seguir mostra roteamento com um modelo de rota mais sofisticado:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-155">The following example shows routing with a more sophisticated route template:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-156">A `/hello/{name:alpha}` seqüência é um **modelo de rota**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-156">The string `/hello/{name:alpha}` is a **route template**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-157">Ele é usado para configurar como o ponto final é correspondido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-157">It is used to configure how the endpoint is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-158">Neste caso, o modelo corresponde:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-158">In this case, the template matches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-159">Uma URL como`/hello/Ryan`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-159">A URL like `/hello/Ryan`</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-160">Qualquer caminho de `/hello/` URL que comece seguido por uma seqüência de caracteres alfabéticos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-160">Any URL path that begins with `/hello/` followed by a sequence of alphabetic characters.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="444c2-161">`:alpha`aplica uma restrição de rota que corresponde apenas a caracteres alfabéticos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-161">`:alpha` applies a route constraint that matches only alphabetic characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-162">[As restrições de rota](#route-constraint-reference) são explicadas mais tarde neste documento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-162">[Route constraints](#route-constraint-reference) are explained later in this document.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-163">O segundo segmento do `{name:alpha}`caminho da URL:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-163">The second segment of the URL path, `{name:alpha}`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-164">Está ligado `name` ao parâmetro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-164">Is bound to the `name` parameter.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-165">É capturado e armazenado em [HttpRequest.RouteValues](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.RouteValues*).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-165">Is captured and stored in [HttpRequest.RouteValues](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.RouteValues*).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-166">O sistema de roteamento de ponto final descrito neste documento é novo a partir de ASP.NET Núcleo 3.0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-166">The endpoint routing system described in this document is new as of ASP.NET Core 3.0.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-167">No entanto, todas as versões do ASP.NET Core suportam o mesmo conjunto de recursos de modelo de rota e restrições de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-167">However, all versions of ASP.NET Core support the same set of route template features and route constraints.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-170">O middleware de autorização pode ser usado com roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-170">The authorization middleware can be used with routing.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-171">Os pontos finais podem ser usados para configurar o comportamento de autorização.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-171">Endpoints can be used to configure authorization behavior.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-172">A <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HealthCheckEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapHealthChecks*> chamada adiciona um ponto final de verificação de saúde.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-172">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HealthCheckEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapHealthChecks*> call adds a health check endpoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-173">O <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthorizationEndpointConventionBuilderExtensions.RequireAuthorization*> acorrentamento a esta chamada anexa uma política de autorização ao ponto final.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-173">Chaining <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthorizationEndpointConventionBuilderExtensions.RequireAuthorization*> on to this call attaches an authorization policy to the endpoint.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-176">Veja qual ponto final `UseRouting`foi selecionado por .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-176">See which endpoint was selected by `UseRouting`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-177">Aplique uma política <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> de autorização antes de despachar para o ponto final.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-177">Apply an authorization policy before <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> dispatches to the endpoint.</span></span>

<a name="metadata"></a>

### <a name="endpoint-metadata"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-178">Metadados de ponto final</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-178">Endpoint metadata</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-179">No exemplo anterior, há dois pontos finais, mas apenas o ponto final da verificação de saúde tem uma política de autorização anexada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-179">In the preceding example, there are two endpoints, but only the health check endpoint has an authorization policy attached.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-180">Se a solicitação corresponder ao `/healthz`ponto final da verificação de saúde, uma verificação de autorização é realizada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-180">If the request matches the health check endpoint, `/healthz`, an authorization check is performed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-181">Isso demonstra que os pontos finais podem ter dados extras anexados a eles.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-181">This demonstrates that endpoints can have extra data attached to them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-182">Esses dados extras são chamados **de metadados**de ponto final:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-182">This extra data is called endpoint **metadata**:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-183">Os metadados podem ser processados por middleware com reconhecimento de roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-183">The metadata can be processed by routing-aware middleware.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-184">Os metadados podem ser de qualquer tipo .NET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-184">The metadata can be of any .NET type.</span></span>

## <a name="routing-concepts"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-185">Conceitos de roteamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-185">Routing concepts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-186">O sistema de roteamento se constrói em cima do pipeline de middleware adicionando o poderoso conceito **de ponto final.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-186">The routing system builds on top of the middleware pipeline by adding the powerful **endpoint** concept.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-187">Os pontos finais representam unidades da funcionalidade do aplicativo que são distintas umas das outras em termos de roteamento, autorização e qualquer número de sistemas do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-187">Endpoints represent units of the app's functionality that are distinct from each other in terms of routing, authorization, and any number of ASP.NET Core's systems.</span></span>

<a name="endpoint"></a>

### <a name="aspnet-core-endpoint-definition"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-188">definição de ponto final do núcleo ASP.NET</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-188">ASP.NET Core endpoint definition</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-189">Um ponto final ASP.NET é:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-189">An ASP.NET Core endpoint is:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-190">Executável: Tem <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.RequestDelegate>um .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-190">Executable: Has a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.RequestDelegate>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-191">Extensível: Tem uma coleção [de Metadados.](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.Metadata*)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-191">Extensible: Has a [Metadata](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.Metadata*) collection.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-192">Selecionável: Opcionalmente, tem [informações de roteamento](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.RoutePattern*).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-192">Selectable: Optionally, has [routing information](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.RoutePattern*).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-193">Enumeração: A coleção de pontos finais pode <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.EndpointDataSource> ser listada recuperando o [DI](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-193">Enumerable: The collection of endpoints can be listed by retrieving the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.EndpointDataSource> from [DI](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-212">O `UseRouting` middleware usa o método [SetEndpoint](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.SetEndpoint*) para anexar o ponto final ao contexto atual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-212">The `UseRouting` middleware uses the [SetEndpoint](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.SetEndpoint*) method to attach the endpoint to the current context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-213">É possível substituir o `UseRouting` middleware por uma lógica personalizada e ainda obter os benefícios de usar endpoints.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-213">It's possible to replace the `UseRouting` middleware with custom logic and still get the benefits of using endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-214">Os pontos finais são primitivos de baixo nível como middleware, e não estão acoplados à implementação de roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-214">Endpoints are a low-level primitive like middleware, and aren't coupled to the routing implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-215">A maioria dos aplicativos `UseRouting` não precisa ser substituída por uma lógica personalizada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-215">Most apps don't need to replace `UseRouting` with custom logic.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-216">O `UseEndpoints` middleware foi projetado para ser usado `UseRouting` em conjunto com o middleware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-216">The `UseEndpoints` middleware is designed to be used in tandem with the `UseRouting` middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-217">A lógica central para executar um ponto final não é complicada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-217">The core logic to execute an endpoint isn't complicated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-218">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.GetEndpoint*> para recuperar o ponto final <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.RequestDelegate> e, em seguida, invoque sua propriedade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-218">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.GetEndpoint*> to retrieve the endpoint, and then invoke its <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.RequestDelegate> property.</span></span>

      * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-226">Muitas vezes toma decisões `UseAuthorization` de `UseCors`segurança, como feito por e .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-226">Often makes security decisions, as done by `UseAuthorization` and `UseCors`.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-227">A combinação de middleware e metadados permite configurar políticas por ponto final.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-227">The combination of middleware and metadata allows configuring policies per-endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-240">Os metadados `AuditPolicyAttribute` da política `Attribute` de auditoria são definidos como um uso mais fácil com frameworks baseados em classe, como controladores e SignalR.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-240">The audit policy metadata `AuditPolicyAttribute` is defined as an `Attribute` for easier use with class-based frameworks such as controllers and SignalR.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-241">Ao usar *a rota para codificar:*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-241">When using *route to code*:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-244">As práticas recomendadas para os tipos de metadados são defini-los como interfaces ou atributos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-244">The best practices for metadata types are to define them either as interfaces or attributes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-245">Interfaces e atributos permitem a reutilização de código.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-245">Interfaces and attributes allow code reuse.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-246">O sistema de metadados é flexível e não impõe limitações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-246">The metadata system is flexible and doesn't impose any limitations.</span></span>

### <a name="comparing-a-terminal-middleware-and-routing"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-247">Comparando um middleware terminal e roteamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-247">Comparing a terminal middleware and routing</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-248">A amostra de código a seguir contrasta usando middleware com o uso de roteamento:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-248">The following code sample contrasts using middleware with using routing:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/TerminalMiddlewareStartup.cs?name=snippet)]

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-249">O estilo de middleware mostrado com `Approach 1:` é **middleware terminal**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-249">The style of middleware shown with `Approach 1:` is **terminal middleware**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-250">Chama-se middleware terminal porque faz uma operação correspondente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-250">It's called terminal middleware because it does a matching operation:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-251">A operação correspondente na `Path == "/"` amostra anterior é `Path == "/Movie"` para o middleware e para o roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-251">The matching operation in the preceding sample is `Path == "/"` for the middleware and `Path == "/Movie"` for routing.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-252">Quando uma correspondência é bem sucedida, ela executa algumas `next` funcionalidades e retorna, em vez de invocar o middleware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-252">When a match is successful, it executes some functionality and returns, rather than invoking the `next` middleware.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-253">Chama-se middleware terminal porque encerra a pesquisa, executa algumas funcionalidades e retorna.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-253">It's called terminal middleware because it terminates the search, executes some functionality, and then returns.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-254">Comparando um middleware terminal e roteamento:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-254">Comparing a terminal middleware and routing:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-255">Ambas as abordagens permitem encerrar o pipeline de processamento:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-255">Both approaches allow terminating the processing pipeline:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-256">Middleware termina o pipeline retornando em `next`vez de invocar .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-256">Middleware terminates the pipeline by returning rather than invoking `next`.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-257">Os pontos finais são sempre terminais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-257">Endpoints are always terminal.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-258">O middleware terminal permite posicionar o middleware em um lugar arbitrário no pipeline:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-258">Terminal middleware allows positioning the middleware at an arbitrary place in the pipeline:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-259">Os pontos finais são <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>executados na posição de .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-259">Endpoints execute at the position of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-260">O middleware terminal permite que o código arbitrário determine quando o middleware corresponde:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-260">Terminal middleware allows arbitrary code to determine when the middleware matches:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-261">O código de correspondência de rota personalizado pode ser verboso e difícil de escrever corretamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-261">Custom route matching code can be verbose and difficult to write correctly.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-262">O roteamento fornece soluções simples para aplicativos típicos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-262">Routing provides straightforward solutions for typical apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-263">A maioria dos aplicativos não requer código de correspondência de rota personalizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-263">Most apps don't require custom route matching code.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-264">Interface de endpoints com `UseAuthorization` `UseCors`middleware como e .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-264">Endpoints interface with middleware such as `UseAuthorization` and `UseCors`.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-265">Utilização de um `UseAuthorization` middleware terminal com ou `UseCors` requer interação manual com o sistema de autorização.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-265">Using a terminal middleware with `UseAuthorization` or `UseCors` requires manual interfacing with the authorization system.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-266">Um [ponto final](#endpoint) define ambos:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-266">An [endpoint](#endpoint) defines both:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-267">Um delegado para processar pedidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-267">A delegate to process requests.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-268">Uma coleção de metadados arbitrários.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-268">A collection of arbitrary metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-269">Os metadados são usados para implementar preocupações transversais com base em políticas e configuração anexadas a cada ponto final.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-269">The metadata is used to implement cross-cutting concerns based on policies and configuration attached to each endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-270">O middleware terminal pode ser uma ferramenta eficaz, mas pode exigir:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-270">Terminal middleware can be an effective tool, but can require:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-271">Uma quantidade significativa de codificação e testes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-271">A significant amount of coding and testing.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-272">Integração manual com outros sistemas para alcançar o nível de flexibilidade desejado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-272">Manual integration with other systems to achieve the desired level of flexibility.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-273">Considere integrar-se com o roteamento antes de escrever um middleware terminal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-273">Consider integrating with routing before writing a terminal middleware.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-274">O middleware de terminal [Map](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index#branch-the-middleware-pipeline) existente <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapWhenExtensions.MapWhen*> que se integra ao Map ou geralmente pode ser transformado em um ponto final de reconhecimento de roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-274">Existing terminal middleware that integrates with [Map](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index#branch-the-middleware-pipeline) or <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapWhenExtensions.MapWhen*> can usually be turned into a routing aware endpoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-275">[MapHealthChecks](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/Middleware/HealthChecks/src/Builder/HealthCheckEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.cs#L16) demonstra o padrão de roteador::</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-275">[MapHealthChecks](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/Middleware/HealthChecks/src/Builder/HealthCheckEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.cs#L16) demonstrates the pattern for router-ware:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-276">Escreva um método <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointRouteBuilder>de extensão em .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-276">Write an extension method on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointRouteBuilder>.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-278">Conecte o middleware ao novo oleoduto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-278">Attach the middleware to the new pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-279">Nesse caso, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HealthCheckApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseHealthChecks*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-279">In this case, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HealthCheckApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseHealthChecks*>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-280"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IApplicationBuilder.Build*>o pipeline de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>middleware em um .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-280"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IApplicationBuilder.Build*> the middleware pipeline into a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-281">Ligue `Map` e forneça o novo oleoduto de middleware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-281">Call `Map` and provide the new middleware pipeline.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-282">Devolva o objeto `Map` construtor fornecido pelo método de extensão.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-282">Return the builder object provided by `Map` from the extension method.</span></span>

<a name="urlm"></a>

### <a name="url-matching"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-289">Correspondência de URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-289">URL matching</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-290">É o processo pelo qual o roteamento corresponde a um pedido de entrada para um [ponto final](#endpoint).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-290">Is the process by which routing matches an incoming request to an [endpoint](#endpoint).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-291">É baseado em dados no caminho url e cabeçalhos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-291">Is based on data in the URL path and headers.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-292">Pode ser estendido para considerar qualquer dado na solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-292">Can be extended to consider any data in the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-293">Quando um middleware de roteamento `Endpoint` é executado, ele define <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpContext> um e os valores de rota para um recurso de [solicitação](xref:fundamentals/request-features) na partir da solicitação atual:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-293">When a routing middleware executes, it sets an `Endpoint` and route values to a [request feature](xref:fundamentals/request-features) on the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpContext> from the current request:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-294">Chamar [httpContext.GetEndpoint](<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.GetEndpoint*>) obtém o ponto final.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-294">Calling [HttpContext.GetEndpoint](<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.GetEndpoint*>) gets the endpoint.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-295">`HttpRequest.RouteValues` obtém a coleção de valores de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-295">`HttpRequest.RouteValues` gets the collection of route values.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-296">[Middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) em execução após o middleware de roteamento pode inspecionar o ponto final e agir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-296">[Middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) running after the routing middleware can inspect the endpoint and take action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-297">Por exemplo, um middleware de autorização pode interrogar a coleta de metadados do ponto final para uma política de autorização.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-297">For example, an authorization middleware can interrogate the endpoint's metadata collection for an authorization policy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-298">Depois que todos os middlewares no pipeline de processamento da solicitação forem executados, o representante do ponto de extremidade selecionado será invocado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-298">After all of the middleware in the request processing pipeline is executed, the selected endpoint's delegate is invoked.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-299">O sistema de roteamento no roteamento de ponto de extremidade é responsável por todas as decisões de expedição.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-299">The routing system in endpoint routing is responsible for all dispatching decisions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-300">Como o middleware aplica políticas com base no ponto final selecionado, é importante que:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-300">Because the middleware applies policies based on the selected endpoint, it's important that:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-301">Qualquer decisão que possa afetar o despacho ou a aplicação de políticas de segurança é tomada dentro do sistema de roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-301">Any decision that can affect dispatching or the application of security policies is made inside the routing system.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-302">Para retrocompatibilidade, quando um delegado de ponto final do Controller ou Razor Pages é executado, as propriedades do [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) são definidas como valores apropriados com base no processamento de solicitação realizado até agora.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-302">For backwards-compatibility, when a Controller or Razor Pages endpoint delegate is executed, the properties of [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) are set to appropriate values based on the request processing performed thus far.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-303">O `RouteContext` tipo será marcado como obsoleto em uma versão futura:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-303">The `RouteContext` type will be marked obsolete in a future release:</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-304">Migrar `RouteData.Values` `HttpRequest.RouteValues`para .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-304">Migrate `RouteData.Values` to `HttpRequest.RouteValues`.</span></span>
> * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-305">Migrar `RouteData.DataTokens` para recuperar [IDataTokensMetadados](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IDataTokensMetadata) a partir dos metadados do ponto final.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-305">Migrate `RouteData.DataTokens` to retrieve [IDataTokensMetadata](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IDataTokensMetadata) from the endpoint metadata.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-306">A correspondência de URL opera em um conjunto de fases configuráveis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-306">URL matching operates in a configurable set of phases.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-307">Em cada fase, a saída é um conjunto de partidas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-307">In each phase, the output is a set of matches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-308">O conjunto de partidas pode ser reduzido ainda mais para a próxima fase.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-308">The set of matches can be narrowed down further by the next phase.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-309">A implementação de roteamento não garante uma ordem de processamento para pontos finais correspondentes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-309">The routing implementation does not guarantee a processing order for matching endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-310">**Todas as** partidas possíveis são processadas de uma só vez.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-310">**All** possible matches are processed at once.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-311">As fases de correspondência de URL ocorrem na seguinte ordem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-311">The URL matching phases occur in the following order.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-312">ASP.NET Core:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-312">ASP.NET Core:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="444c2-313">Processa o caminho de URL em relação ao conjunto de pontos finais e seus modelos de rota, coletando **todas as** correspondências.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-313">Processes the URL path against the set of endpoints and their route templates, collecting **all** of the matches.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="444c2-314">Pega a lista anterior e remove correspondências que falham com as restrições de rota aplicadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-314">Takes the preceding list and removes matches that fail with route constraints applied.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="444c2-315">Pega a lista anterior e remove as correspondências que falham no conjunto de instâncias [do MatcherPolicy.](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.MatcherPolicy)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-315">Takes the preceding list and removes matches that fail the set of [MatcherPolicy](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.MatcherPolicy) instances.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="444c2-316">Usa o [EndpointSelector](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Matching.EndpointSelector) para tomar uma decisão final da lista anterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-316">Uses the [EndpointSelector](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Matching.EndpointSelector) to make a final decision from the preceding list.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-317">A lista de pontos finais é priorizada de acordo com:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-317">The list of endpoints is prioritized according to:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-318">O [RouteEndpoint.Order](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.Order*)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-318">The [RouteEndpoint.Order](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.Order*)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-319">A [precedência do modelo de rota](#rtp)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-319">The [route template precedence](#rtp)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-320">Todos os pontos finais correspondentes são <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Matching.EndpointSelector> processados em cada fase até que o seja atingido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-320">All matching endpoints are processed in each phase until the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Matching.EndpointSelector> is reached.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-321">A `EndpointSelector` fase final.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-321">The `EndpointSelector` is the final phase.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-322">Ele escolhe o ponto final de maior prioridade das partidas como a melhor partida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-322">It chooses the highest priority endpoint from the matches as the best match.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-323">Se houver outras partidas com a mesma prioridade da melhor partida, uma exceção ambígua de partida é lançada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-323">If there are other matches with the same priority as the best match, an ambiguous match exception is thrown.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-324">A precedência da rota é calculada com base em um modelo de rota **mais específico** que recebe uma prioridade maior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-324">The route precedence is computed based on a **more specific** route template being given a higher priority.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-325">Por exemplo, considere `/hello` os `/{message}`modelos e:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-325">For example, consider the templates `/hello` and `/{message}`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-326">Ambos correspondem `/hello`ao caminho da URL .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-326">Both match the URL path `/hello`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-327">`/hello`é mais específica e, portanto, maior prioridade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-327">`/hello`  is more specific and therefore higher priority.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-328">Em geral, a precedência de rota faz um bom trabalho de escolher a melhor combinação para os tipos de esquemas de URL usados na prática.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-328">In general, route precedence does a good job of choosing the best match for the kinds of URL schemes used in practice.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-329">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.Order> somente quando necessário para evitar uma ambiguidade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-329">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.Order> only when necessary to avoid an ambiguity.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-330">Devido aos tipos de extensibilidade proporcionados pelo roteamento, não é possível que o sistema de roteamento calcule antecipadamente as rotas ambíguas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-330">Due to the kinds of extensibility provided by routing, it isn't possible for the routing system to compute ahead of time the ambiguous routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-331">Considere um exemplo, como `/{message:alpha}` os `/{message:int}`modelos de rota e:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-331">Consider an example such as the route templates `/{message:alpha}` and `/{message:int}`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-332">A `alpha` restrição corresponde apenas a caracteres alfabéticos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-332">The `alpha` constraint matches only alphabetic characters.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-333">A `int` restrição corresponde apenas aos números.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-333">The `int` constraint matches only numbers.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-334">Esses modelos têm a mesma precedência de rota, mas não há uma única URL que ambos correspondam.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-334">These templates have the same route precedence, but there's no single URL they both match.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-335">Se o sistema de roteamento relatasse um erro de ambiguidade na inicialização, ele bloquearia esse caso de uso válido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-335">If the routing system reported an ambiguity error at startup, it would block this valid use case.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
>
> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-336">A ordem das <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> operações internas não influencia o comportamento do roteamento, com uma exceção.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-336">The order of operations inside <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> doesn't influence the behavior of routing, with one exception.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-337"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllerRoute*>e <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MvcAreaRouteBuilderExtensions.MapAreaRoute*> atribuir automaticamente um valor de ordem aos seus pontos finais com base na ordem que eles são invocados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-337"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllerRoute*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MvcAreaRouteBuilderExtensions.MapAreaRoute*> automatically assign an order value to their endpoints based on the order they are invoked.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-338">Isso simula o comportamento de longa data dos controladores sem que o sistema de roteamento forneça as mesmas garantias que as implementações de roteamento mais antigas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-338">This simulates long-time behavior of controllers without the routing system providing the same guarantees as older routing implementations.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-339">Na implementação legado do roteamento, é possível implementar a extensibilidade de roteamento que tenha uma dependência da ordem em que as rotas são processadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-339">In the legacy implementation of routing, it's possible to implement routing extensibility that has a dependency on the order in which routes are processed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-340">Roteamento de ponto final no ASP.NET Núcleo 3.0 e posteriores:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-340">Endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 3.0 and later:</span></span>
> 
> * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-341">Não tem um conceito de rotas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-341">Doesn't have a concept of routes.</span></span>
> * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-342">Não fornece garantias de pedidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-342">Doesn't provide ordering guarantees.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-343">Todos os pontos finais são processados ao mesmo tempo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-343">All endpoints are processed at once.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-344">Se isso significa que você está preso usando o sistema de roteamento legado, [abra um problema do GitHub para assistência](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/issues).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-344">If this means you're stuck using the legacy routing system, [open a GitHub issue for assistance](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/issues).</span></span>

<a name="rtp"></a>

### <a name="route-template-precedence-and-endpoint-selection-order"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-345">Precedência do modelo de rota e ordem de seleção de ponto final</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-345">Route template precedence and endpoint selection order</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-346">[Precedência do modelo de rota](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/master/src/Http/Routing/src/Template/RoutePrecedence.cs#L16) é um sistema que atribui a cada modelo de rota um valor com base no quão específico ele é.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-346">[Route template precedence](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/master/src/Http/Routing/src/Template/RoutePrecedence.cs#L16) is a system that assigns each route template a value based on how specific it is.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-347">Precedência do modelo de rota:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-347">Route template precedence:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-348">Evita a necessidade de ajustar a ordem dos pontos finais em casos comuns.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-348">Avoids the need to adjust the order of endpoints in common cases.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-349">Tentativas de corresponder às expectativas de senso comum do comportamento de roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-349">Attempts to match the common-sense expectations of routing behavior.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-350">Por exemplo, considere `/Products/List` `/Products/{id}`modelos e .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-350">For example, consider templates `/Products/List` and `/Products/{id}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-351">Seria razoável supor `/Products/List` que é `/Products/{id}` uma combinação `/Products/List`melhor do que para o caminho da URL .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-351">It would be reasonable to assume that `/Products/List` is a better match than `/Products/{id}` for the URL path `/Products/List`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-352">Os trabalhos porque `/List` o segmento literal é considerado com `/{id}`melhor precedência do que o segmento de parâmetros .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-352">The works because the literal segment `/List` is considered to have better precedence than the parameter segment `/{id}`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-353">Os detalhes de como a precedência funciona são acoplados à forma como os modelos de rota são definidos:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-353">The details of how precedence works are coupled to how route templates are defined:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-354">Modelos com mais segmentos são considerados mais específicos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-354">Templates with more segments are considered more specific.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-355">Um segmento com texto literal é considerado mais específico do que um segmento de parâmetros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-355">A segment with literal text is considered more specific than a parameter segment.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-356">Um segmento de parâmetros com restrição é considerado mais específico do que um sem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-356">A parameter segment with a constraint is considered more specific than one without.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-357">Um segmento complexo é considerado específico como um segmento de parâmetros com restrição.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-357">A complex segment is considered as specific as a parameter segment with a constraint.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-358">Pegar todos os parâmetros são os menos específicos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-358">Catch all parameters are the least specific.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-359">Consulte o [código-fonte no GitHub](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/master/src/Http/Routing/src/Template/RoutePrecedence.cs#L189) para obter uma referência de valores exatos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-359">See the [source code on GitHub](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/master/src/Http/Routing/src/Template/RoutePrecedence.cs#L189) for a reference of exact values.</span></span>

<a name="lg"></a>

### <a name="url-generation-concepts"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-360">Conceitos de geração de URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-360">URL generation concepts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-361">Geração de URL:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-361">URL generation:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-362">É o processo pelo qual o roteamento pode criar um caminho de URL baseado em um conjunto de valores de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-362">Is the process by which routing can create a URL path based on a set of route values.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-363">Permite uma separação lógica entre os pontos finais e os URLs que os acessam.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-363">Allows for a logical separation between endpoints and the URLs that access them.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-364">O roteamento de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> ponto final inclui a API.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-364">Endpoint routing includes the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-365">`LinkGenerator`é um serviço singleton disponível na [DI](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-365">`LinkGenerator` is a singleton service available from [DI](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-366">A `LinkGenerator` API pode ser usada fora do contexto de uma solicitação de execução.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-366">The `LinkGenerator` API can be used outside of the context of an executing request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-367">[Mvc.IUrlHelper](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper) e cenários <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper>que dependem , como [Tag Helpers,](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro)AJUDADORES `LinkGenerator` HTML e Resultados de [Ação,](xref:mvc/controllers/actions)usam a API internamente para fornecer recursos de geração de links.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-367">[Mvc.IUrlHelper](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper) and scenarios that rely on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper>, such as [Tag Helpers](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro), HTML Helpers, and [Action Results](xref:mvc/controllers/actions), use the `LinkGenerator` API internally to provide link generating capabilities.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-368">O gerador de link é respaldado pelo conceito de um **endereço** e **esquemas de endereço**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-368">The link generator is backed by the concept of an **address** and **address schemes**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-369">Um esquema de endereço é uma maneira de determinar os pontos de extremidade que devem ser considerados para a geração de link.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-369">An address scheme is a way of determining the endpoints that should be considered for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-370">Por exemplo, os cenários de valores de nome e rota de rota que muitos usuários estão familiarizados com os controladores e páginas de barbear são implementados como um esquema de endereço.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-370">For example, the route name and route values scenarios many users are familiar with from controllers and Razor Pages are implemented as an address scheme.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-371">O gerador de links pode ser ligado a controladores e páginas de barbear através dos seguintes métodos de extensão:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-371">The link generator can link to controllers and Razor Pages via the following extension methods:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.ControllerLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetPathByAction*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.ControllerLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetUriByAction*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.PageLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetPathByPage*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.PageLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetUriByPage*>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-372">Sobrecargas desses métodos aceitam argumentos que incluem o `HttpContext`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-372">Overloads of these methods accept arguments that include the `HttpContext`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-373">Esses métodos são funcionalmente equivalentes ao [Url.Action](xref:System.Web.Mvc.UrlHelper.Action*) e [url.Page,](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.UrlHelperExtensions.Page*)mas oferecem flexibilidade e opções adicionais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-373">These methods are functionally equivalent to [Url.Action](xref:System.Web.Mvc.UrlHelper.Action*) and [Url.Page](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.UrlHelperExtensions.Page*), but offer additional flexibility and options.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-374">Os `GetPath*` métodos são `Url.Action` mais `Url.Page`semelhantes e, na forma, geram um URI contendo um caminho absoluto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-374">The `GetPath*` methods are most similar to `Url.Action` and `Url.Page`, in that they generate a URI containing an absolute path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-375">Os métodos `GetUri*` sempre geram um URI absoluto que contém um esquema e um host.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-375">The `GetUri*` methods always generate an absolute URI containing a scheme and host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-376">Os métodos que aceitam um `HttpContext` geram um URI no contexto da solicitação em execução.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-376">The methods that accept an `HttpContext` generate a URI in the context of the executing request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-377">Os valores da rota [ambiente,](#ambient) o caminho base da URL, o esquema e o host da solicitação de execução são usados, a menos que seja substituído.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-377">The [ambient](#ambient) route values, URL base path, scheme, and host from the executing request are used unless overridden.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-378"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> é chamado com um endereço.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-378"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> is called with an address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-379">A geração de um URI ocorre em duas etapas:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-379">Generating a URI occurs in two steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="444c2-380">Um endereço é associado a uma lista de pontos de extremidade que correspondem ao endereço.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-380">An address is bound to a list of endpoints that match the address.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="444c2-381">O <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.RoutePattern> de cada ponto de extremidade é avaliado até que seja encontrado um padrão de rota correspondente aos valores fornecidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-381">Each endpoint's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.RoutePattern> is evaluated until a route pattern that matches the supplied values is found.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-382">A saída resultante é combinada com as outras partes de URI fornecidas ao gerador de link e é retornada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-382">The resulting output is combined with the other URI parts supplied to the link generator and returned.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-383">Os métodos fornecidos pelo <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> dão suporte a funcionalidades de geração de link padrão para qualquer tipo de endereço.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-383">The methods provided by <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> support standard link generation capabilities for any type of address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-384">A maneira mais conveniente de usar o gerador de links é através de métodos de extensão que executam operações para um tipo de endereço específico:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-384">The most convenient way to use the link generator is through extension methods that perform operations for a specific address type:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-385">Método de extensão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-385">Extension Method</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-386">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-386">Description</span></span> |
| ---------------- | ----------- |
| <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetPathByAddress*> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-387">Gera um URI com um caminho absoluto com base nos valores fornecidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-387">Generates a URI with an absolute path based on the provided values.</span></span> |
| <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetUriByAddress*> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-388">Gera um URI absoluto com base nos valores fornecidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-388">Generates an absolute URI based on the provided values.</span></span>             |

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-389">Preste atenção às seguintes implicações da chamada de métodos <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-389">Pay attention to the following implications of calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> methods:</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-390">Use métodos de extensão de `GetUri*` com cuidado em uma configuração de aplicativo que não valide o cabeçalho `Host` das solicitações de entrada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-390">Use `GetUri*` extension methods with caution in an app configuration that doesn't validate the `Host` header of incoming requests.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-391">Se `Host` o cabeçalho das solicitações recebidas não for validado, a entrada de solicitação não confiável pode ser enviada de volta ao cliente em URIs em uma exibição ou página.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-391">If the `Host` header of incoming requests isn't validated, untrusted request input can be sent back to the client in URIs in a view or page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-392">Recomendamos que todos os aplicativos de produção configurem seu servidor para validar o cabeçalho `Host` com os valores válidos conhecidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-392">We recommend that all production apps configure their server to validate the `Host` header against known valid values.</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-393">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> com cuidado no middleware em combinação com `Map` ou `MapWhen`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-393">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> with caution in middleware in combination with `Map` or `MapWhen`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-394">`Map*` altera o caminho base da solicitação em execução, o que afeta a saída da geração de link.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-394">`Map*` changes the base path of the executing request, which affects the output of link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-395">Todas as APIs de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> permitem a especificação de um caminho base.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-395">All of the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> APIs allow specifying a base path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-396">Especifique um caminho `Map*` base vazio para desfazer o efeito na geração de links.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-396">Specify an empty base path to undo the `Map*` affect on link generation.</span></span>
