## <a name="route-template-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-400">Referência de modelo de rota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-400">Route template reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-401">Os tokens dentro `{}` definem parâmetros de rota vinculados se a rota for combinada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-401">Tokens within `{}` define route parameters that are bound if the route is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-402">Mais de um parâmetro de rota pode ser definido em um segmento de rota, mas os parâmetros de rota devem ser separados por um valor literal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-402">More than one route parameter can be defined in a route segment, but route parameters  must be separated by a literal value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-403">Por exemplo, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` não é uma rota válida, já que não há nenhum valor literal entre `{controller}` e `{action}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-403">For example, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` isn't a valid route, since there's no literal value between `{controller}` and `{action}`.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="444c2-404">Os parâmetros de rota devem ter um nome e podem ter atributos adicionais especificados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-404">Route parameters must have a name and may have additional attributes specified.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-405">Um texto literal diferente dos parâmetros de rota (por exemplo, `{id}`) e do separador de caminho `/` precisa corresponder ao texto na URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-405">Literal text other than route parameters (for example, `{id}`) and the path separator `/` must match the text in the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-406">A correspondência de texto não diferencia maiúsculas de minúsculas e se baseia na representação decodificada do caminho de URLs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-406">Text matching is case-insensitive and based on the decoded representation of the URLs path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-407">Para combinar com um parâmetro `{` de `}`rota literal delimitador ou , escape do delimitador repetindo o caractere.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-407">To match a literal route parameter delimiter `{` or `}`, escape the delimiter by repeating the character.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-408">Por `{{` exemplo, ou `}}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-408">For example `{{` or `}}`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-409">Asterisco `*` ou duplo `**`asterisco:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-409">Asterisk `*` or double asterisk `**`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-410">Pode ser usado como um prefixo para um parâmetro de rota para se ligar ao resto do URI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-410">Can be used as a prefix to a route parameter to bind to the rest of the URI.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-411">São chamados de parâmetros **de captura.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-411">Are called a **catch-all** parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-412">Por exemplo `blog/{**slug}`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-412">For example, `blog/{**slug}`:</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-413">Corresponde a qualquer `/blog` URI que comece e tenha qualquer valor a segui-lo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-413">Matches any URI that starts with `/blog` and has any value following it.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-414">O valor `/blog` a seguir é atribuído ao valor da rota [de lesma.](https://developer.mozilla.org/docs/Glossary/Slug)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-414">The value following `/blog` is assigned to the [slug](https://developer.mozilla.org/docs/Glossary/Slug) route value.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-415">Os parâmetros catch-all também podem corresponder à cadeia de caracteres vazia.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-415">Catch-all parameters can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-416">O parâmetro catch-all escapa dos caracteres apropriados quando a rota é `/` usada para gerar uma URL, incluindo caracteres separadores de caminho.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-416">The catch-all parameter escapes the appropriate characters when the route is used to generate a URL, including path separator `/` characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-417">Por exemplo, a rota `foo/{*path}` com valores de rota `{ path = "my/path" }` gera `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-417">For example, the route `foo/{*path}` with route values `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-418">Observe o escape da barra invertida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-418">Note the escaped forward slash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-419">Para fazer a viagem de ida e volta dos caracteres separadores de caminho, use o prefixo do parâmetro da rota `**`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-419">To round-trip path separator characters, use the `**` route parameter prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-420">A rota `foo/{**path}` com `{ path = "my/path" }` gera `foo/my/path`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-420">The route `foo/{**path}` with `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my/path`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-421">Padrões de URL que tentam capturar um nome de arquivo com uma extensão de arquivo opcional apresentam considerações adicionais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-421">URL patterns that attempt to capture a file name with an optional file extension have additional considerations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-422">Por exemplo, considere o modelo `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-422">For example, consider the template `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-423">Quando existem valores para `filename` e `ext`, ambos os valores são populados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-423">When values for both `filename` and `ext` exist, both values are populated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-424">Se apenas um `filename` valor para existir na URL, `.` a rota corresponde porque a trilha é opcional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-424">If only a value for `filename` exists in the URL, the route matches because the trailing `.` is  optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-425">As URLs a seguir correspondem a essa rota:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-425">The following URLs match this route:</span></span>

* `/files/myFile.txt`
* `/files/myFile`

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-426">Os parâmetros de rota podem ter **valores padrão**, designados pela especificação do valor padrão após o nome do parâmetro separado por um sinal de igual (`=`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-426">Route parameters may have **default values** designated by specifying the default value after the parameter name separated by an equals sign (`=`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-427">Por exemplo, `{controller=Home}` define `Home` como o valor padrão de `controller`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-427">For example, `{controller=Home}` defines `Home` as the default value for `controller`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-428">O valor padrão é usado se nenhum valor está presente na URL para o parâmetro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-428">The default value is used if no value is present in the URL for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-429">Os parâmetros de rota são opcionais anexando um ponto de interrogação (`?`) ao final do nome do parâmetro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-429">Route parameters are made optional by appending a question mark (`?`) to the end of the parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-430">Por exemplo, `id?`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-430">For example, `id?`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-431">A diferença entre valores opcionais e parâmetros de rota padrão é:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-431">The difference between optional values and default route parameters is:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-432">Um parâmetro de rota com um valor padrão sempre produz um valor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-432">A route parameter with a default value always produces a value.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-433">Um parâmetro opcional tem um valor apenas quando um valor é fornecido pela URL de solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-433">An optional parameter has a value only when a value is provided by the request URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-434">Os parâmetros de rota podem ter restrições que precisam corresponder ao valor de rota associado da URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-434">Route parameters may have constraints that must match the route value bound from the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-435">A `:` adição e o nome de restrição após o nome do parâmetro de rota especifica monsofam uma restrição inline em um parâmetro de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-435">Adding `:` and constraint name after the route parameter name specifies an inline constraint on a route parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-436">Se a restrição exigir argumentos, eles ficarão entre parênteses `(...)` após o nome da restrição.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-436">If the constraint requires arguments, they're enclosed in parentheses `(...)` after the constraint name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-437">Várias *restrições inline* podem ser `:` especificadas anexando outro nome de restrição.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-437">Multiple *inline constraints* can be specified by appending another `:` and constraint name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-438">O nome da restrição e os argumentos são passados para o serviço <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> para criar uma instância de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> a ser usada no processamento de URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-438">The constraint name and arguments are passed to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> service to create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> to use in URL processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-439">Por exemplo, o modelo de rota `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` especifica uma restrição `minlength` com o argumento `10`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-439">For example, the route template `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifies a `minlength` constraint with the argument `10`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-440">Para obter mais informações sobre as restrições de rota e uma lista das restrições fornecidas pela estrutura, confira a seção [Referência de restrição de rota](#route-constraint-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-440">For more information on route constraints and a list of the constraints provided by the framework, see the [Route constraint reference](#route-constraint-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-441">Os parâmetros de rota também podem ter transformadores de parâmetros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-441">Route parameters may also have parameter transformers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-442">Os transformadores de parâmetro transformam o valor de um parâmetro ao gerar links e ações e páginas correspondentes a URLs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-442">Parameter transformers transform a parameter's value when generating links and matching actions and pages to URLs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-443">Como as restrições, os transformadores de parâmetros podem ser `:` adicionados em linha a um parâmetro de rota adicionando um nome e transformador após o nome do parâmetro de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-443">Like constraints, parameter transformers can be added inline to a route parameter by adding a `:` and transformer name after the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-444">Por exemplo, o modelo de rota `blog/{article:slugify}` especifica um transformador `slugify`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-444">For example, the route template `blog/{article:slugify}` specifies a `slugify` transformer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-445">Para obter mais informações sobre transformadores de parâmetro, confira a seção [Referência de transformador de parâmetro](#parameter-transformer-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-445">For more information on parameter transformers, see the [Parameter transformer reference](#parameter-transformer-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-446">A tabela a seguir demonstra modelos de rota de exemplo e seu comportamento:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-446">The following table demonstrates example route templates and their behavior:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-447">Modelo de rota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-447">Route Template</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-448">URI de correspondência de exemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-448">Example Matching URI</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-449">O URI de solicitação&hellip;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-449">The request URI&hellip;</span></span>                                                    |
| ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `hello`                                  | `/hello`                | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-450">Somente corresponde ao caminho único `/hello`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-450">Only matches the single path `/hello`.</span></span>                                     |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-451">Faz a correspondência e define `Page` como `Home`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-451">Matches and sets `Page` to `Home`.</span></span>                                         |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/Contact`              | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-452">Faz a correspondência e define `Page` como `Contact`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-452">Matches and sets `Page` to `Contact`.</span></span>                                      |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/List`        | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-453">É mapeado para o controlador `Products` e a ação `List`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-453">Maps to the `Products` controller and `List` action.</span></span>                       |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/Details/123` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-454">Mapas para `Products` o `Details` controlador`id` e ação com conjunto para 123.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-454">Maps to the `Products` controller and  `Details` action with`id` set to 123.</span></span> |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-455">Mapas para `Home` o `Index` controlador e método.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-455">Maps to the `Home` controller and `Index` method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-456">`id` é ignorado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-456">`id` is ignored.</span></span>        |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/Products`         | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-457">Mapas para `Products` o `Index` controlador e método.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-457">Maps to the `Products` controller and `Index` method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-458">`id` é ignorado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-458">`id` is ignored.</span></span>        |

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-459">Em geral, o uso de um modelo é a abordagem mais simples para o roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-459">Using a template is generally the simplest approach to routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-460">Restrições e padrões também podem ser especificados fora do modelo de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-460">Constraints and defaults can also be specified outside the route template.</span></span>

### <a name="complex-segments"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-461">Segmentos complexos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-461">Complex segments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-462">Segmentos complexos são processados combinando delimitadores literais da direita para a esquerda de forma [não gananciosa.](#greedy)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-462">Complex segments are processed by matching up literal delimiters from right to left in a [non-greedy](#greedy) way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-463">Por exemplo, `[Route("/a{b}c{d}")]` é um segmento complexo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-463">For example, `[Route("/a{b}c{d}")]` is a complex segment.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="444c2-464">Segmentos complexos funcionam de uma maneira particular que deve ser entendida para usá-los com sucesso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-464">Complex segments work in a particular way that must be understood to use them successfully.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-465">O exemplo nesta seção demonstra por que segmentos complexos só funcionam bem quando o texto delimitador não aparece dentro dos valores dos parâmetros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-465">The example in this section demonstrates why complex segments only really work well when the delimiter text doesn't appear inside the parameter values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-466">Usar um [regex](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expressions) e, em seguida, extrair manualmente os valores é necessário para casos mais complexos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-466">Using a [regex](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expressions) and then manually extracting the values is needed for more complex cases.</span></span>

[!INCLUDE[](~/includes/regex.md)]

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-467">Este é um resumo das etapas que o `/a{b}c{d}` roteamento `/abcd`executa com o modelo e o caminho url .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-467">This is a summary of the steps that routing performs with the template `/a{b}c{d}` and the URL path `/abcd`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-468">O `|` é usado para ajudar a visualizar como o algoritmo funciona:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-468">The `|` is used to help visualize how the algorithm works:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-469">O primeiro literal, da `c`direita para a esquerda, é.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-469">The first literal, right to left, is `c`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-470">Assim `/abcd` é pesquisado pela `/ab|c|d`direita e encontra.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-470">So `/abcd` is searched from right and finds `/ab|c|d`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-471">Tudo à direita`d`( ) agora é compatível `{d}`com o parâmetro de rota .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-471">Everything to the right (`d`) is now matched to the route parameter `{d}`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-472">O próximo literal, da `a`direita para a esquerda, é.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-472">The next literal, right to left, is `a`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-473">Então `/ab|c|d` é pesquisado começando de onde `a` paramos, então é encontrado. `/|a|b|c|d`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-473">So `/ab|c|d` is searched starting where we left off, then `a` is found `/|a|b|c|d`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-474">O valor à`b`direita ( ) agora é `{b}`compatível com o parâmetro de rota .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-474">The value to the right (`b`) is now matched to the route parameter `{b}`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-475">Não há texto restante e nenhum modelo de rota restante, então este é um jogo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-475">There is no remaining text and no remaining route template, so this is a match.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-476">Aqui está um exemplo de um caso `/a{b}c{d}` negativo usando `/aabcd`o mesmo modelo e o caminho da URL .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-476">Here's an example of a negative case using the same template `/a{b}c{d}` and the URL path `/aabcd`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-477">O `|` é usado para ajudar a visualizar como o algoritmo funciona.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-477">The `|` is used to help visualize how the algorithm works.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-478">Este caso não é compatível, o que é explicado pelo mesmo algoritmo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-478">This case isn't a match, which is explained by the same algorithm:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-479">O primeiro literal, da `c`direita para a esquerda, é.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-479">The first literal, right to left, is `c`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-480">Assim `/aabcd` é pesquisado pela `/aab|c|d`direita e encontra.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-480">So `/aabcd` is searched from right and finds `/aab|c|d`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-481">Tudo à direita`d`( ) agora é compatível `{d}`com o parâmetro de rota .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-481">Everything to the right (`d`) is now matched to the route parameter `{d}`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-482">O próximo literal, da `a`direita para a esquerda, é.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-482">The next literal, right to left, is `a`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-483">Então `/aab|c|d` é pesquisado começando de onde `a` paramos, então é encontrado. `/a|a|b|c|d`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-483">So `/aab|c|d` is searched starting where we left off, then `a` is found `/a|a|b|c|d`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-484">O valor à`b`direita ( ) agora é `{b}`compatível com o parâmetro de rota .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-484">The value to the right (`b`) is now matched to the route parameter `{b}`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-485">Neste ponto há texto `a`restante, mas o algoritmo ficou sem modelo de rota para analisar, então isso não é compatível.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-485">At this point there is remaining text `a`, but the algorithm has run out of route template to parse, so this is not a match.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-486">Uma vez que o algoritmo de correspondência não é [ganancioso:](#greedy)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-486">Since the matching algorithm is [non-greedy](#greedy):</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-487">Corresponde à menor quantidade de texto possível em cada etapa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-487">It matches the smallest amount of text possible in each step.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-488">Qualquer caso em que o valor de limitador aparece dentro dos valores do parâmetro resulta em não correspondência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-488">Any case where the delimiter value appears inside the parameter values results in not matching.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-489">Expressões regulares fornecem muito mais controle sobre seu comportamento correspondente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-489">Regular expressions provide much more control over their matching behavior.</span></span>

<a name="greedy"></a>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-490">Correspondência gananciosa, também conhecida como [partida preguiçosa,](https://wikipedia.org/wiki/Regular_expression#Lazy_matching)combina com a maior seqüência possível.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-490">Greedy matching, also know as [lazy matching](https://wikipedia.org/wiki/Regular_expression#Lazy_matching), matches the largest possible string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-491">Não-ganancioso combina com a menor seqüência possível.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-491">Non-greedy matches the smallest possible string.</span></span>

## <a name="route-constraint-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-492">Referência de restrição de rota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-492">Route constraint reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-493">As restrições de rota são executadas quando ocorre uma correspondência com a URL de entrada e é criado um token do caminho da URL em valores de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-493">Route constraints execute when a match has occurred to the incoming URL and the URL path is tokenized into route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-494">As restrições de rota geralmente inspecionam o valor da rota associado através do modelo de rota e tomam uma decisão verdadeira ou falsa sobre se o valor é aceitável.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-494">Route constraints generally inspect the route value associated via the route template and make a true or false decision about whether the value is acceptable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-495">Algumas restrições da rota usam dados fora do valor de rota para considerar se a solicitação pode ser encaminhada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-495">Some route constraints use data outside the route value to consider whether the request can be routed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-496">Por exemplo, a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> pode aceitar ou rejeitar uma solicitação de acordo com o verbo HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-496">For example, the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> can accept or reject a request based on its HTTP verb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-497">As restrições são usadas em solicitações de roteamento e na geração de link.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-497">Constraints are used in routing requests and link generation.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-498">Não use restrições para a validação de entrada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-498">Don't use constraints for input validation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-499">Se as restrições forem usadas para validação `404` de entrada, a entrada inválida resultará em uma resposta não encontrada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-499">If constraints are used for input validation, invalid input results in a `404` Not Found response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-500">A entrada inválida `400` deve produzir uma solicitação ruim com uma mensagem de erro apropriada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-500">Invalid input should produce a `400` Bad Request with an appropriate error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-501">As restrições de rota são usadas para desfazer a ambiguidade entre rotas semelhantes, não para validar as entradas de uma rota específica.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-501">Route constraints are used to disambiguate similar routes, not to validate the inputs for a particular route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-502">A tabela a seguir demonstra as restrições de rota de exemplo e seu comportamento esperado:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-502">The following table demonstrates example route constraints and their expected behavior:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-503">restrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-503">constraint</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-504">Exemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-504">Example</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-505">Correspondências de exemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-505">Example Matches</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-506">Observações</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-506">Notes</span></span> |
| ---------- | ------- | --------------- | ----- |
| `int` | `{id:int}` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-507">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-507">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-508">Corresponde a qualquer inteiro</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-508">Matches any integer</span></span> |
| `bool` | `{active:bool}` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-509">`true`, `FALSE`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-509">`true`, `FALSE`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-510">`true` Fósforos `false`ou .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-510">Matches `true` or `false`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-511">Não diferenciam maiúsculas de minúsculas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-511">Case-insensitive</span></span> |
| `datetime` | `{dob:datetime}` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-512">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-512">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-513">Corresponde a `DateTime` um valor válido na cultura invariante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-513">Matches a valid `DateTime` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-514">Veja o aviso anterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-514">See preceding warning.</span></span> |

| `regex(expression)` | `{ssn:regex(^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$)}` | `123-45-6789` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-535">A corda deve corresponder à expressão regular.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-535">String must match the regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-536">Veja dicas sobre como definir uma expressão regular.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-536">See tips about defining a regular expression.</span></span> |
| `required` | `{name:required}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-537">Usado para impor que um valor não parâmetro está presente durante a geração de URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-537">Used to enforce that a non-parameter value is present during URL generation</span></span> |

[!INCLUDE[](~/includes/regex.md)]

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-538">Restrições múltiplas e delimitadas de cólon podem ser aplicadas a um único parâmetro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-538">Multiple, colon delimited constraints can be applied to a single parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-539">Por exemplo, a restrição a seguir restringe um parâmetro para um valor inteiro de 1 ou maior:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-539">For example, the following constraint restricts a parameter to an integer value of 1 or greater:</span></span>

```csharp
[Route("users/{id:int:min(1)}")]
public User GetUserById(int id) { }
```

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-540">As restrições de rota que verificam a URL e são convertidas para um tipo CLR sempre usam a cultura invariante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-540">Route constraints that verify the URL and are converted to a CLR type always use the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-541">Por exemplo, conversão para `int` o `DateTime`tipo CLR ou .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-541">For example, conversion to the CLR type `int` or `DateTime`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-542">Essas restrições assumem que a URL não é localizável.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-542">These constraints assume that the URL is not localizable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-543">As restrições de rota fornecidas pela estrutura não modificam os valores armazenados nos valores de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-543">The framework-provided route constraints don't modify the values stored in route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-544">Todos os valores de rota analisados com base na URL são armazenados como cadeias de caracteres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-544">All route values parsed from the URL are stored as strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-545">Por exemplo, a restrição `float` tenta converter o valor de rota em um float, mas o valor convertido é usado somente para verificar se ele pode ser convertido em um float.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-545">For example, the `float` constraint attempts to convert the route value to a float, but the converted value is used only to verify it can be converted to a float.</span></span>

### <a name="regular-expressions-in-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-546">Expressões regulares em restrições</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-546">Regular expressions in constraints</span></span>

[!INCLUDE[](~/includes/regex.md)]

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-547">Expressões regulares podem ser especificadas como `regex(...)` restrições inline usando a restrição de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-547">Regular expressions can be specified as inline constraints using the `regex(...)` route constraint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-548">Os métodos <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllerRoute*> na família também aceitam um objeto literal de restrições.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-548">Methods in the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllerRoute*> family also accept an object literal of constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-549">Se essa forma for usada, os valores das cordas são interpretados como expressões regulares.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-549">If that form is used, string values are interpreted as regular expressions.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-552">A estrutura do ASP.NET Core adiciona `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` ao construtor de expressão regular.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-552">The ASP.NET Core framework adds `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` to the regular expression constructor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-553">Confira <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> para obter uma descrição desses membros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-553">See <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> for a description of these members.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-554">Expressões regulares usam delimitadores e tokens semelhantes aos usados pelo roteamento e pela linguagem C#.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-554">Regular expressions use delimiters and tokens similar to those used by routing and the C# language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-555">Os tokens de expressão regular precisam ter escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-555">Regular expression tokens must be escaped.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-556">Para usar a `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` expressão regular em uma restrição inline, use um dos seguintes:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-556">To use the regular expression `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` in an inline constraint, use one of the following:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-557">Substitua `\` os caracteres `\\` fornecidos na seqüência como caracteres no arquivo de origem C# para escapar do caractere de fuga de `\` seqüência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-557">Replace `\` characters provided in the string as `\\` characters in the C# source file in order to escape the `\` string escape character.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-558">[Literals de cordas verbatim](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-558">[Verbatim string literals](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-559">Para escapar `{`dos caracteres delimitadores do parâmetro de roteamento, `{{` `}}` `[[` `]]` `}` `[` `]`o dobro dos caracteres na expressão, por exemplo, mas, .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-559">To escape routing parameter delimiter characters `{`, `}`, `[`, `]`, double the characters in the expression, for example, `{{`, `}}`, `[[`, `]]`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-560">A tabela a seguir mostra uma expressão regular e sua versão fugitiva:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-560">The following table shows a regular expression and its escaped version:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-561">Expressão regular</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-561">Regular expression</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-562">Escapou da expressão regular</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-562">Escaped regular expression</span></span>     |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` | `^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$` |
| `^[a-z]{2}$`          | `^[[a-z]]{{2}}$`               |

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-563">Expressões regulares usadas no roteamento geralmente começam com o `^` caractere e correspondem à posição inicial da string.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-563">Regular expressions used in routing often start with the `^` character and match the starting position of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-564">As expressões geralmente `$` terminam com o personagem e combinam com o final da seqüência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-564">The expressions often end with the `$` character and match the end of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-565">Os `^` `$` caracteres garantem que a expressão regular corresponda a todo o valor do parâmetro de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-565">The `^` and `$` characters ensure that the regular expression matches the entire route parameter value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-566">Sem `^` `$` os caracteres, a expressão regular corresponde a qualquer substring dentro da seqüência, o que muitas vezes é indesejável.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-566">Without the `^` and `$` characters, the regular expression matches any substring within the string, which is often undesirable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-567">A tabela a seguir fornece exemplos e explica por que eles correspondem ou não correspondem:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-567">The following table provides examples and explains why they match or fail to match:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-568">Expression</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-568">Expression</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-569">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-569">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-570">Corresponder a</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-570">Match</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-571">Comentário</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-571">Comment</span></span>               |
| ------------ | --------- | :---: |  -------------------- |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-572">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-572">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-573">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-573">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-574">A subcadeia de caracteres corresponde</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-574">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-575">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-575">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-576">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-576">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-577">A subcadeia de caracteres corresponde</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-577">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-578">mz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-578">mz</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-579">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-579">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-580">Corresponde à expressão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-580">Matches expression</span></span>    |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-581">MZ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-581">MZ</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-582">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-582">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-583">Não diferencia maiúsculas de minúsculas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-583">Not case sensitive</span></span>    |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-584">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-584">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-585">Não</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-585">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-586">Confira `^` e `$` acima</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-586">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-587">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-587">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-588">Não</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-588">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-589">Confira `^` e `$` acima</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-589">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-590">Para saber mais sobre a sintaxe de expressões regulares, confira [Expressões regulares do .NET Framework](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-590">For more information on regular expression syntax, see [.NET Framework Regular Expressions](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-591">Para restringir um parâmetro a um conjunto conhecido de valores possíveis, use uma expressão regular.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-591">To constrain a parameter to a known set of possible values, use a regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-592">Por exemplo, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` apenas corresponde o valor da rota `action` a `list`, `get` ou `create`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-592">For example, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` only matches the `action` route value to `list`, `get`, or `create`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-593">Se passada para o dicionário de restrições, a cadeia de caracteres `^(list|get|create)$` é equivalente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-593">If passed into the constraints dictionary, the string `^(list|get|create)$` is equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-594">Restrições que são passadas no dicionário de restrições que não correspondem a uma das restrições conhecidas também são tratadas como expressões regulares.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-594">Constraints that are passed in the constraints dictionary that don't match one of the known constraints are also treated as regular expressions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-595">As restrições que são passadas dentro de um modelo que não correspondem a uma das restrições conhecidas não são tratadas como expressões regulares.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-595">Constraints that are passed  within a template that don't match one of the known constraints are not treated as regular expressions.</span></span>

### <a name="custom-route-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-596">Restrições de rota personalizadas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-596">Custom route constraints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-597">As restrições de rota personalizadas <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> podem ser criadas implementando a interface.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-597">Custom route constraints can be created by implementing the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-598">A `IRouteConstraint` interface <xref:System.Web.Routing.IRouteConstraint.Match*>contém `true` , que retorna `false` se a restrição estiver satisfeita e de outra forma.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-598">The `IRouteConstraint` interface contains <xref:System.Web.Routing.IRouteConstraint.Match*>, which returns `true` if the constraint is satisfied and `false` otherwise.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-599">Restrições de rota personalizadas raramente são necessárias.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-599">Custom route constraints are rarely needed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-600">Antes de implementar uma restrição de rota personalizada, considere alternativas, como a vinculação do modelo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-600">Before implementing a custom route constraint, consider alternatives, such as model binding.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-601">Para usar `IRouteConstraint`um personalizado, o tipo de restrição de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> rota deve ser registrado com o aplicativo no contêiner de serviço.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-601">To use a custom `IRouteConstraint`, the route constraint type must be registered with the app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in the service container.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-602">O `ConstraintMap` é um dicionário que mapeia as chaves de restrição de rota para implementações de `IRouteConstraint` que validam essas restrições.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-602">A `ConstraintMap` is a dictionary that maps route constraint keys to `IRouteConstraint` implementations that validate those constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-603">É possível atualizar o `ConstraintMap` do aplicativo no `Startup.ConfigureServices` como parte de uma chamada [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) ou configurando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> diretamente com `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-603">An app's `ConstraintMap` can be updated in `Startup.ConfigureServices` either as part of a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) call or by configuring <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directly with `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-604">Por exemplo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-604">For example:</span></span>

## <a name="parameter-transformer-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-615">Referência de parâmetro de transformador</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-615">Parameter transformer reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-616">Transformadores de parâmetro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-616">Parameter transformers:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-617">Execute ao gerar um <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>link usando .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-617">Execute when generating a link using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-618">Implementar <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IOutboundParameterTransformer?displayProperty=fullName>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-618">Implement <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IOutboundParameterTransformer?displayProperty=fullName>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-619">São configurados usando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-619">Are configured using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-620">Usam o valor de rota do parâmetro e o transformam em um novo valor de cadeia de caracteres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-620">Take the parameter's route value and transform it to a new string value.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-621">Resultam no uso do valor transformado no link gerado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-621">Result in using the transformed value in the generated link.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-622">Por exemplo, um transformador de parâmetro `slugify` personalizado em padrão de rota `blog\{article:slugify}` com `Url.Action(new { article = "MyTestArticle" })` gera `blog\my-test-article`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-622">For example, a custom `slugify` parameter transformer in route pattern `blog\{article:slugify}` with `Url.Action(new { article = "MyTestArticle" })` generates `blog\my-test-article`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-630">ASP.NET Core fornece convenções de API para o uso de transformadores de parâmetros com rotas geradas:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-630">ASP.NET Core provides API conventions for using parameter transformers with generated routes:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-631">A <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.RouteTokenTransformerConvention?displayProperty=fullName> convenção MVC aplica um transformador de parâmetro especificado a todas as rotas de atributos no aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-631">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.RouteTokenTransformerConvention?displayProperty=fullName> MVC convention applies a specified parameter transformer to all attribute routes in the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-632">O transformador de parâmetro transforma os tokens de rota do atributo conforme elas são substituídas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-632">The parameter transformer transforms attribute route tokens as they are replaced.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-633">Para obter mais informações, confira [Usar um transformador de parâmetro para personalizar a substituição de token](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-token-replacement).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-633">For more information, see [Use a parameter transformer to customize token replacement](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-token-replacement).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-634">Razor Pages <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.PageRouteTransformerConvention> usa a convenção da API.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-634">Razor Pages uses the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.PageRouteTransformerConvention> API convention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-635">Essa convenção aplica um transformador de parâmetro especificado a todas as Razor Pages descobertas automaticamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-635">This convention applies a specified parameter transformer to all automatically discovered Razor Pages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-636">O transformador de parâmetro transforma os segmentos de nome de arquivo e pasta de rotas do Razor Pages.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-636">The parameter transformer transforms the folder and file name segments of Razor Pages routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-637">Para obter mais informações, confira [Usar um transformador de parâmetros para personalizar rotas de página](xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-page-routes).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-637">For more information, see [Use a parameter transformer to customize page routes](xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-page-routes).</span></span>

<a name="ugr"></a>

## <a name="url-generation-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-638">Referência de geração de URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-638">URL generation reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-639">Esta seção contém uma referência para o algoritmo implementado pela geração de URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-639">This section contains a reference for the algorithm implemented by URL generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-640">Na prática, os exemplos mais complexos de geração de URL usam controladores ou páginas de barbear.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-640">In practice, most complex examples of URL generation use controllers or Razor Pages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-641">Consulte [o roteamento nos controladores](xref:mvc/controllers/routing) para obter informações adicionais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-641">See  [routing in controllers](xref:mvc/controllers/routing) for additional information.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-642">O processo de geração de URL começa com uma chamada para [LinkGenerator.GetPathByAddress](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetPathByAddress*) ou um método semelhante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-642">The URL generation process begins with a call to [LinkGenerator.GetPathByAddress](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetPathByAddress*) or a similar method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-643">O método é fornecido com um endereço, um conjunto de valores `HttpContext`de rota e, opcionalmente, informações sobre a solicitação atual de .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-643">The method is provided with an address, a set of route values, and optionally information about the current request from `HttpContext`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-644">O primeiro passo é usar o endereço para resolver [`IEndpointAddressScheme<TAddress>`](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointAddressScheme`1) um conjunto de pontos finais do candidato usando um que corresponda ao tipo do endereço.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-644">The first step is to use the address to resolve a set of candidate endpoints using an [`IEndpointAddressScheme<TAddress>`](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointAddressScheme`1) that matches the address's type.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-645">Uma vez que o conjunto de candidatos é encontrado pelo esquema de endereços, os pontos finais são ordenados e processados iterativamente até que uma operação de geração de URL seja bem sucedida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-645">Once of set of candidates is found by the address scheme, the endpoints are ordered and processed iteratively until a URL generation operation succeeds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-646">A geração de URL **não** verifica as ambiguidades, o primeiro resultado retornado é o resultado final.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-646">URL generation does **not** check for ambiguities, the first result returned is the final result.</span></span>

### <a name="troubleshooting-url-generation-with-logging"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-647">Solucionando a geração de URL com o registro</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-647">Troubleshooting URL generation with logging</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-648">O primeiro passo para solucionar `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing` problemas na geração de URL é definir o nível de registro de . `TRACE`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-648">The first step in troubleshooting URL generation is setting the logging level of `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing` to `TRACE`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-649">`LinkGenerator`registra muitos detalhes sobre seu processamento que podem ser úteis para solucionar problemas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-649">`LinkGenerator` logs many details about its processing which can be useful to troubleshoot problems.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-650">Consulte [a referência de geração de URL](#ugr) para obter detalhes sobre a geração de URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-650">See [URL generation reference](#ugr) for details on URL generation.</span></span>

### <a name="addresses"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-651">Endereços</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-651">Addresses</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-652">Os endereços são o conceito na geração de URL usado para vincular uma chamada ao gerador de links a um conjunto de pontos finais do candidato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-652">Addresses are the concept in URL generation used to bind a call into the link generator to a set of candidate endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-653">Os endereços são um conceito extensível que vêm com duas implementações por padrão:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-653">Addresses are an extensible concept that come with two implementations by default:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-654">Usando o nome`string`do ponto *final* () como endereço:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-654">Using *endpoint name* (`string`) as the address:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-655">Fornece funcionalidade semelhante ao nome da rota do MVC.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-655">Provides similar functionality to MVC's route name.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-656">Usa <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointNameMetadata> o tipo de metadados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-656">Uses the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointNameMetadata> metadata type.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-657">Resolve a seqüência fornecida contra os metadados de todos os pontos finais registrados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-657">Resolves the provided string against the metadata of all registered endpoints.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-658">Abre uma exceção na inicialização se vários pontos finais usarem o mesmo nome.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-658">Throws an exception on startup if multiple endpoints use the same name.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-659">Recomendado para uso geral fora dos controladores e páginas de barbear.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-659">Recommended for general-purpose use outside of controllers and Razor Pages.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-660">Usando *valores de rota* (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteValuesAddress>) como endereço:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-660">Using *route values* (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteValuesAddress>) as the address:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-661">Fornece funcionalidade semelhante aos controladores e à geração de URL legado razor pages.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-661">Provides similar functionality to controllers and Razor Pages legacy URL generation.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-662">Muito complexo para estender e depurar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-662">Very complex to extend and debug.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-663">Fornece a implementação usada por `IUrlHelper`, Tag Helpers, HTML Helpers, Action Results, etc.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-663">Provides the implementation used by `IUrlHelper`, Tag Helpers, HTML Helpers, Action Results, etc.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-664">O papel do esquema de endereço é fazer a associação entre o endereço e os pontos finais correspondentes por critérios arbitrários:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-664">The role of the address scheme is to make the association between the address and matching endpoints by arbitrary criteria:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-665">O esquema de nome de ponto final executa uma pesquisa básica do dicionário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-665">The endpoint name scheme performs a basic dictionary lookup.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-666">O esquema de valores de rota tem um complexo melhor subconjunto de algoritmo de conjunto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-666">The route values scheme has a complex best subset of set algorithm.</span></span>

<a name="ambient"></a>

### <a name="ambient-values-and-explicit-values"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-667">Valores ambientais e valores explícitos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-667">Ambient values and explicit values</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-668">A partir da solicitação atual, o roteamento `HttpContext.Request.RouteValues`acessa os valores de rota da solicitação atual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-668">From the current request, routing accesses the route values of the current request `HttpContext.Request.RouteValues`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-669">Os valores associados à solicitação atual são chamados de **valores ambientais.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-669">The values associated with the current request are referred to as the **ambient values**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-670">Para fins de clareza, a documentação refere-se aos valores de rota repassados aos métodos como **valores explícitos.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-670">For the purpose of clarity, the documentation refers to the route values passed in to methods as **explicit values**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-671">O exemplo a seguir mostra valores ambientais e valores explícitos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-671">The following example shows ambient values and explicit values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-672">Fornece valores ambientais a partir da `{ id = 17, }`solicitação atual e valores explícitos: :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-672">It provides ambient values from the current request and explicit values: `{ id = 17, }`:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/Controllers/WidgetController.cs?name=snippet)]

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-673">O código anterior:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-673">The preceding code:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-674">Retorna `/Widget/Index/17`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-674">Returns `/Widget/Index/17`</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-675">Fica <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> via [DI](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-675">Gets <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> via [DI](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-676">O código a seguir não fornece `{ controller = "Home", action = "Subscribe", id = 17, }`valores ambientais e valores explícitos: :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-676">The following code provides no ambient values and explicit values: `{ controller = "Home", action = "Subscribe", id = 17, }`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-681">`/Gadget/Edit/17`é devolvido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-681">`/Gadget/Edit/17` is returned.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-682"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ControllerBase.Url>recebe <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper>o .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-682"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ControllerBase.Url> gets the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper>.</span></span>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.UrlHelperExtensions.Action*>
