<span data-ttu-id="444c2-686">O código `url` anterior `/Edit/17` define-se para quando a Página de navalha de edição contém a seguinte diretiva de página:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-686">The preceding code sets `url` to  `/Edit/17` when the Edit Razor Page contains the following page directive:</span></span>

 `@page "{id:int}"`

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-687">Se a página Editar não `"{id:int}"` contiver `url` `/Edit?id=17`o modelo de rota, será .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-687">If the Edit page doesn't contain the `"{id:int}"` route template, `url` is `/Edit?id=17`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-688">O comportamento dos MVC's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> adiciona uma camada de complexidade além das regras descritas aqui:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-688">The behavior of MVC's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> adds a layer of complexity in addition to the rules described here:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-689">`IUrlHelper`sempre fornece os valores de rota da solicitação atual como valores ambientais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-689">`IUrlHelper` always provides the route values from the current request as ambient values.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-690">[O IUrlHelper.Action](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.UrlHelperExtensions.Action*) sempre `action` `controller` copia os valores atuais e de rota como valores explícitos, a menos que substituído pelo desenvolvedor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-690">[IUrlHelper.Action](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.UrlHelperExtensions.Action*) always copies the current `action` and `controller` route values as explicit values unless overridden by the developer.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-691">[IUrlHelper.Page](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.UrlHelperExtensions.Page*) sempre copia `page` o valor de rota atual como um valor explícito, a menos que substituído.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-691">[IUrlHelper.Page](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.UrlHelperExtensions.Page*) always copies the current `page` route value as an explicit value unless overridden.</span></span> <!--by the user-->
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-692">`IUrlHelper.Page`sempre substitui o `handler` valor `null` de rota atual com como valores explícitos, a menos que substituído.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-692">`IUrlHelper.Page` always overrides the current `handler` route value with `null` as an explicit values unless overridden.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-693">Os usuários são muitas vezes surpreendidos pelos detalhes comportamentais dos valores ambientais, porque o MVC parece não seguir suas próprias regras.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-693">Users are often surprised by the behavioral details of ambient values, because MVC doesn't seem to follow its own rules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-694">Por razões históricas e de `action`compatibilidade, certos valores de rota, tais como , `controller`, `page`e `handler` têm seu próprio comportamento de caso especial.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-694">For historical and compatibility reasons, certain route values such as `action`, `controller`, `page`, and `handler` have their own special-case behavior.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-695">A funcionalidade equivalente fornecida `LinkGenerator.GetPathByAction` `LinkGenerator.GetPathByPage` e duplica essas anomalias de `IUrlHelper` compatibilidade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-695">The equivalent functionality provided by `LinkGenerator.GetPathByAction` and `LinkGenerator.GetPathByPage` duplicates these anomalies of `IUrlHelper` for compatibility.</span></span>

### <a name="url-generation-process"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-696">Processo de geração de URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-696">URL generation process</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-697">Uma vez que o conjunto de pontos finais do candidato é encontrado, o algoritmo de geração de URL:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-697">Once the set of candidate endpoints are found, the URL generation algorithm:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-698">Processa os pontos finais de forma iterativa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-698">Processes the endpoints iteratively.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-699">Retorna o primeiro resultado bem sucedido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-699">Returns the first successful result.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-700">A primeira etapa deste processo é chamada **de invalidação de valor de rota**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-700">The first step in this process is called **route value invalidation**.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="444c2-701">A invalidação do valor da rota é o processo pelo qual o roteamento decide quais valores de rota dos valores ambientais devem ser usados e quais devem ser ignorados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-701">Route value invalidation is the process by which routing decides which route values from the ambient values should be used and which should be ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-702">Cada valor ambiente é considerado e combinado com os valores explícitos, ou ignorado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-702">Each ambient value is considered and either combined with the explicit values, or ignored.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-703">A melhor maneira de pensar sobre o papel dos valores ambientais é que eles tentam salvar os desenvolvedores de aplicativos digitando, em alguns casos comuns.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-703">The best way to think about the role of ambient values is that they attempt to save application developers typing, in some common cases.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-704">Tradicionalmente, os cenários em que os valores ambientais são úteis estão relacionados ao MVC:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-704">Traditionally, the scenarios where ambient values are helpful are related to MVC:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-705">Ao vincular-se a outra ação no mesmo controlador, o nome do controlador não precisa ser especificado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-705">When linking to another action in the same controller, the controller name doesn't need to be specified.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-706">Ao vincular a outro controlador na mesma área, o nome da área não precisa ser especificado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-706">When linking to another controller in the same area, the area name doesn't need to be specified.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-707">Ao vincular-se ao mesmo método de ação, os valores de rota não precisam ser especificados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-707">When linking to the same action method, route values don't need to be specified.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-708">Ao vincular a outra parte do aplicativo, você não quer carregar valores de rota que não têm significado nessa parte do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-708">When linking to another part of the app, you don't want to carry over route values that have no meaning in that part of the app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-709">Chamadas `LinkGenerator` para `IUrlHelper` ou `null` esse retorno geralmente são causadas por não entender a invalidação do valor da rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-709">Calls to `LinkGenerator` or `IUrlHelper` that return `null` are usually caused by not understanding route value invalidation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-710">Solucionar problemas na invalidação do valor da rota especificando explicitamente mais valores de rota para ver se isso resolve o problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-710">Troubleshoot route value invalidation by explicitly specifying more of the route values to see if that solves the problem.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-711">A invalidação de valor de rota funciona com o pressuposto de que o esquema de URL do aplicativo é hierárquico, com uma hierarquia formada da esquerda para a direita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-711">Route value invalidation works on the assumption that the app's URL scheme is hierarchical, with a hierarchy formed from left-to-right.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-712">Considere o modelo `{controller}/{action}/{id?}` básico de rota do controlador para ter uma noção intuitiva de como isso funciona na prática.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-712">Consider the basic controller route template `{controller}/{action}/{id?}` to get an intuitive sense of how this works in practice.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-713">Uma **alteração** para um valor **invalida** todos os valores de rota que aparecem à direita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-713">A **change** to a value **invalidates** all of the route values that appear to the right.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-714">Isso reflete a suposição sobre hierarquia.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-714">This reflects the assumption about hierarchy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-715">Se o aplicativo tiver `id`um valor ambiente para , e `controller`a operação especificar um valor diferente para:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-715">If the app has an ambient value for `id`, and the operation specifies a different value for the `controller`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-716">`id`não será reutilizado `{controller}` porque está à `{id?}`esquerda de .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-716">`id` won't be reused because `{controller}` is to the left of `{id?}`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-717">Alguns exemplos demonstram esse princípio:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-717">Some examples demonstrating this principle:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-718">Se os valores explícitos contiverem um valor para `id`, o valor ambiente para `id` é ignorado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-718">If the explicit values contain a value for `id`, the ambient value for `id` is ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-719">Os valores `controller` `action` ambientais para e podem ser usados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-719">The ambient values for `controller` and `action` can be used.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-720">Se os valores explícitos contiverem um valor para `action`, qualquer valor ambiente para `action` é ignorado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-720">If the explicit values contain a value for `action`, any ambient value for `action` is ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-721">Os valores `controller` ambientais podem ser usados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-721">The ambient values for `controller` can be used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-722">Se o valor `action` explícito for for `action`different `id` do valor ambiente para , o valor não será usado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-722">If the explicit value for `action` is different from the ambient value for `action`, the `id` value won't be used.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="444c2-723">Se o valor `action` explícito for for o `action`mesmo `id` que o valor ambiente para , o valor pode ser usado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-723">If the explicit value for `action` is the same as the ambient value for `action`, the `id` value can be used.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-724">Se os valores explícitos contiverem um valor para `controller`, qualquer valor ambiente para `controller` é ignorado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-724">If the explicit values contain a value for `controller`, any ambient value for `controller` is ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-725">Se o valor `controller` explícito for for `controller`different `action` do `id` valor ambiente para , os valores e não serão usados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-725">If the explicit value for `controller` is different from the ambient value for `controller`, the `action` and `id` values won't be used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-726">Se o valor `controller` explícito for é o `controller`mesmo `action` `id` do valor ambiente para , os valores podem ser usados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-726">If the explicit value for `controller` is the same as the ambient value for `controller`, the `action` and `id` values can be used.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-727">Esse processo é ainda mais complicado pela existência de rotas de atributos e rotas convencionais dedicadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-727">This process is further complicated by the existence of attribute routes and dedicated conventional routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-728">Controller rotas convencionais, como `{controller}/{action}/{id?}` especificar uma hierarquia usando parâmetros de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-728">Controller conventional routes such as `{controller}/{action}/{id?}` specify a hierarchy using route parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-729">Para [rotas convencionais dedicadas](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#dcr) e [rotas de atributo](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#ar) para controladores e páginas de barbear:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-729">For [dedicated conventional routes](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#dcr) and [attribute routes](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#ar) to controllers and Razor Pages:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-730">Há uma hierarquia de valores de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-730">There is a hierarchy of route values.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-731">Eles não aparecem no modelo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-731">They don't appear in the template.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-732">Para esses casos, a geração de URL define o conceito **de valores necessários.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-732">For these cases, URL generation defines the **required values** concept.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-733">Os pontos finais criados pelos controladores e páginas de barbear têm valores exigidos especificados que permitem que a invalidação de valor de rota funcione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-733">Endpoints created by controllers and Razor Pages have required values specified that allow route value invalidation to work.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-734">O algoritmo de invalidação de valor de rota em detalhes:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-734">The route value invalidation algorithm in detail:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-735">Os nomes de valor necessários são combinados com os parâmetros de rota e, em seguida, processados da esquerda para a direita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-735">The required value names are combined with the route parameters, then processed from left-to-right.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-736">Para cada parâmetro, o valor ambiente e o valor explícito são comparados:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-736">For each parameter, the ambient value and explicit value are compared:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-737">Se o valor ambiente e o valor explícito forem os mesmos, o processo continua.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-737">If the ambient value and explicit value are the same, the process continues.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-738">Se o valor ambiente estiver presente e o valor explícito não estiver, o valor ambiente será usado ao gerar a URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-738">If the ambient value is present and the explicit value isn't, the ambient value is used when generating the URL.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-739">Se o valor ambiente não estiver presente e o valor explícito estiver, rejeite o valor ambiente e todos os valores ambientais subsequentes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-739">If the ambient value isn't present and the explicit value is, reject the ambient value and all subsequent ambient values.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-740">Se o valor ambiente e o valor explícito estiverem presentes, e os dois valores forem diferentes, rejeite o valor ambiente e todos os valores ambientais subsequentes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-740">If the ambient value and the explicit value are present, and the two values are different, reject the ambient value and all subsequent ambient values.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-741">Neste ponto, a operação de geração de URL está pronta para avaliar as restrições de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-741">At this point, the URL generation operation is ready to evaluate route constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-742">O conjunto de valores aceitos é combinado com os valores padrão do parâmetro, que é fornecido às restrições.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-742">The set of accepted values is combined with the parameter default values, which is provided to constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-743">Se as restrições passarem, a operação continua.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-743">If the constraints all pass, the operation continues.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-744">Em seguida, os **valores aceitos** podem ser usados para expandir o modelo de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-744">Next, the **accepted values** can be used to expand the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-745">O modelo de rota é processado:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-745">The route template is processed:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-746">Da esquerda para a direita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-746">From left-to-right.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-747">Cada parâmetro tem seu valor aceito substituído.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-747">Each parameter has its accepted value substituted.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-748">Com os seguintes casos especiais:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-748">With the following special cases:</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-749">Se os valores aceitos perderem um valor e o parâmetro tiver um valor padrão, o valor padrão será usado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-749">If the accepted values is missing a value and the parameter has a default value, the default value is used.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-750">Se os valores aceitos estão faltando um valor e o parâmetro é opcional, o processamento continua.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-750">If the accepted values is missing a value and the parameter is optional, processing continues.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-751">Se algum parâmetro de rota à direita de um parâmetro opcional ausente tiver um valor, a operação falhará.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-751">If any route parameter to the right of a missing optional parameter has a value, the operation fails.</span></span>
  * <!-- review default-valued parameters optional parameters --> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-752">Parâmetros de valor padrão contíguos e parâmetros opcionais são colapsados sempre que possível.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-752">Contiguous default-valued parameters and optional parameters are collapsed where possible.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-753">Valores explicitamente fornecidos que não correspondem a um segmento da rota são adicionados à seqüência de consultas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-753">Values explicitly provided that don't match a segment of the route are added to the query string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-754">A tabela a seguir mostra o resultado do uso do modelo de rota `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-754">The following table shows the result when using the route template `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-755">Valores de ambiente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-755">Ambient Values</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-756">Valores explícitos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-756">Explicit Values</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-757">Result</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-757">Result</span></span>                  |
| ---------------------------------- | -------------------------------------- | ----------------------- |
| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-758">controlador = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-758">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-759">ação = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-759">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-760">controlador = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-760">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-761">controlador = "Order", ação = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-761">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span></span> | `/Order/About`          |

### <a name="problems-with-route-value-invalidation"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-766">Problemas com a invalidação do valor da rota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-766">Problems with route value invalidation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-767">A partir de ASP.NET O Core 3.0, alguns esquemas de geração de URL usados no início ASP.NET versões Core não funcionam bem com a geração de URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-767">As of ASP.NET Core 3.0, some URL generation schemes used in earlier ASP.NET Core versions don't work well with URL generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-768">A equipe do ASP.NET Core planeja adicionar recursos para atender a essas necessidades em um lançamento futuro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-768">The ASP.NET Core team plans to add features to address these needs in a future release.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-769">Por enquanto, a melhor solução é usar roteamento legado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-769">For now the best solution is to use legacy routing.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-770">O código a seguir mostra um exemplo de um esquema de geração de URL que não é suportado pelo roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-770">The following code shows an example of a URL generation scheme that's not supported by routing.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-771">No código anterior, `culture` o parâmetro de rota é usado para localização.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-771">In the preceding code, the `culture` route parameter is used for localization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-772">O desejo é `culture` ter o parâmetro sempre aceito como valor ambiente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-772">The desire is to have the `culture` parameter always accepted as an ambient value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-773">No entanto, o `culture` parâmetro não é aceito como um valor ambiente devido à forma como os valores necessários funcionam:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-773">However, the `culture` parameter is not accepted as an ambient value because of the way required values work:</span></span>

## <a name="host-matching-in-routes-with-requirehost"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-783">Correspondência de host em rotas com RequireHost</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-783">Host matching in routes with RequireHost</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-784"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingEndpointConventionBuilderExtensions.RequireHost*>aplica uma restrição à rota que requer o host especificado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-784"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingEndpointConventionBuilderExtensions.RequireHost*> applies a constraint to the route which requires the specified host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-785">O `RequireHost` parâmetro [ou [Host]](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.HostAttribute) pode ser:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-785">The `RequireHost` or [[Host]](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.HostAttribute) parameter can be:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-786">Anfitrião: `www.domain.com`, `www.domain.com` combina com qualquer porta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-786">Host: `www.domain.com`, matches `www.domain.com` with any port.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-787">Hospede com `*.domain.com`curinga: , fósforos `www.domain.com`, `subdomain.domain.com`, ou `www.subdomain.domain.com` em qualquer porta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-787">Host with wildcard: `*.domain.com`, matches `www.domain.com`, `subdomain.domain.com`, or `www.subdomain.domain.com` on any port.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-788">Porta: `*:5000`, corresponde a porta 5000 com qualquer host.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-788">Port: `*:5000`, matches port 5000 with any host.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-789">Host e `www.domain.com:5000` porta: ou `*.domain.com:5000`, corresponde host e porta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-789">Host and port: `www.domain.com:5000` or `*.domain.com:5000`, matches host and port.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-790">Vários parâmetros podem `RequireHost` ser `[Host]`especificados usando ou .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-790">Multiple parameters can be specified using `RequireHost` or `[Host]`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-791">A restrição corresponde aos hosts válidos para qualquer um dos parâmetros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-791">The constraint  matches hosts valid for any of the parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-792">Por `[Host("domain.com", "*.domain.com")]` exemplo, `domain.com` `www.domain.com`fósforos `subdomain.domain.com`e.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-792">For example, `[Host("domain.com", "*.domain.com")]` matches `domain.com`, `www.domain.com`, and `subdomain.domain.com`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-793">O código `RequireHost` a seguir é necessário para exigir o host especificado na rota:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-793">The following code uses `RequireHost` to require the specified host on the route:</span></span>

## <a name="performance-guidance-for-routing"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-798">Orientação de desempenho para roteamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-798">Performance guidance for routing</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-799">A maior parte do roteamento foi atualizada em ASP.NET Núcleo 3.0 para aumentar o desempenho.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-799">Most of routing was updated in ASP.NET Core 3.0 to increase performance.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-800">Quando um aplicativo tem problemas de desempenho, muitas vezes é suspeito o roteamento como o problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-800">When an app has performance problems, routing is often suspected as the problem.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-801">A razão pela qual o roteamento é que estruturas como controladores e páginas de barbear relatam a quantidade de tempo gasto dentro da estrutura em suas mensagens de registro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-801">The reason routing is suspected is that frameworks like controllers and Razor Pages report the amount of time spent inside the framework in their logging messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-802">Quando há uma diferença significativa entre o tempo relatado pelos controladores e o tempo total da solicitação:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-802">When there's a significant difference between the time reported by controllers and the total time of the request:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-803">Os desenvolvedores eliminam seu código de aplicativo como a fonte do problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-803">Developers eliminate their app code as the source of the problem.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-804">É comum assumir que o encaminhamento é a causa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-804">It's common to assume routing is the cause.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-805">O roteamento é testado com desempenho usando milhares de pontos finais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-805">Routing is performance tested using thousands of endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-806">É improvável que um aplicativo típico encontre um problema de desempenho apenas por ser muito grande.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-806">It's unlikely that a typical app will encounter a performance problem just by being too large.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-807">A causa raiz mais comum do desempenho de roteamento lento é geralmente um middleware personalizado mal comportado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-807">The most common root cause of slow routing performance is usually a badly-behaving custom middleware.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-808">Esta amostra de código a seguir demonstra uma técnica básica para reduzir a fonte de atraso:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-808">This following code sample demonstrates a basic technique for narrowing down the source of delay:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/StartupDelay.cs?name=snippet)]

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-809">Para o roteamento do tempo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-809">To time routing:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-810">Intercale cada middleware com uma cópia do middleware de tempo mostrado no código anterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-810">Interleave each middleware with a copy of the timing middleware shown in the preceding code.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-812">Esta é uma maneira básica de reduzir o atraso quando é `10ms`significativo, por exemplo, mais do que .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-812">This is a basic way to narrow down the delay when it's significant, for example, more than `10ms`.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="444c2-813">Subtraindo `Time 2` `Time 1` dos relatórios o `UseRouting` tempo gasto dentro do middleware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-813">Subtracting `Time 2` from `Time 1` reports the time spent inside the `UseRouting` middleware.</span></span>

### <a name="potentially-expensive-routing-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-815">Recursos de roteamento potencialmente caros</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-815">Potentially expensive routing features</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-816">A lista a seguir fornece algumas informações sobre os recursos de roteamento que são relativamente caros em comparação com os modelos básicos de rota:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-816">The following list provides some insight into routing features that are relatively expensive compared with basic route templates:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-817">Expressões regulares: É possível escrever expressões regulares que são complexas, ou têm tempo de execução longo com uma pequena quantidade de entrada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-817">Regular expressions: It's possible to write regular expressions that are complex, or have long running time with a small amount of input.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-818">Segmentos`{x}-{y}-{z}`complexos ( ):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-818">Complex segments (`{x}-{y}-{z}`):</span></span> 
  * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-819">São significativamente mais caros do que analisar um segmento de caminho de URL regular.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-819">Are significantly more expensive than parsing a regular URL path segment.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-820">Resultando em muito mais substrings sendo alocados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-820">Result in many more substrings being allocated.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="444c2-821">A lógica complexa do segmento não foi atualizada em ASP.NET atualização de desempenho de roteamento do Core 3.0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-821">The complex segment logic was not updated in ASP.NET Core 3.0 routing performance update.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-822">Acesso síncrono de dados: Muitos aplicativos complexos têm acesso ao banco de dados como parte de seu roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-822">Synchronous data access: Many complex apps have database access as part of their routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-823">ASP.NET Core 2.2 e o roteamento anterior podem não fornecer os pontos de extensibilidade certos para suportar o roteamento de acesso ao banco de dados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-823">ASP.NET Core 2.2 and earlier routing might not provide the right extensibility points to support database access routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-824">Por exemplo, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ActionConstraints.IActionConstraint> e são síncronos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-824">For example, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>, and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ActionConstraints.IActionConstraint> are synchronous.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-825">Pontos de extensibilidade como <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.MatcherPolicy> e <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.EndpointSelectorContext> são assíncronos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-825">Extensibility points such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.MatcherPolicy> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.EndpointSelectorContext> are asynchronous.</span></span>

## <a name="guidance-for-library-authors"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-826">Orientação para autores de bibliotecas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-826">Guidance for library authors</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-827">Esta seção contém orientações para autores de bibliotecas que se baseiam em cima do roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-827">This section contains guidance for library authors building on top of routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-828">Esses detalhes visam garantir que os desenvolvedores de aplicativos tenham uma boa experiência usando bibliotecas e frameworks que estendem o roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-828">These details are intended to ensure that app developers have a good experience using libraries and frameworks that extend routing.</span></span>

### <a name="define-endpoints"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-829">Definir pontos finais</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-829">Define endpoints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-830">Para criar uma estrutura que use roteamento para correspondência de URL, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>comece definindo uma experiência de usuário que se baseia em cima de .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-830">To create a framework that uses routing for URL matching, start by defining a user experience that builds on top of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-831">**DO** construa <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointRouteBuilder>em cima de .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-831">**DO** build on top of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointRouteBuilder>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-832">Isso permite que os usuários componham sua estrutura com outros recursos ASP.NET Core sem confusão.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-832">This allows users to compose your framework with other ASP.NET Core features without confusion.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-833">Cada modelo ASP.NET Core inclui roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-833">Every ASP.NET Core template includes routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-834">Assuma que o roteamento está presente e familiar para os usuários.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-834">Assume routing is present and familiar for users.</span></span>

```csharp
app.UseEndpoints(endpoints =>
{
    // Your framework
    endpoints.MapMyFramework(...);

    endpoints.MapHealthChecks("/healthz");
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-835">**DO** devolva um tipo `MapMyFramework(...)` de concreto <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IEndpointConventionBuilder>selado de uma chamada para que implemente .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-835">**DO** return a sealed concrete type from a call to `MapMyFramework(...)` that implements <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IEndpointConventionBuilder>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-836">A `Map...` maioria dos métodos-estrutura seguem esse padrão.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-836">Most framework `Map...` methods follow this pattern.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-837">A `IEndpointConventionBuilder` interface:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-837">The `IEndpointConventionBuilder` interface:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-838">Permite a composição de metadados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-838">Allows composability of metadata.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-839">É alvo de uma variedade de métodos de extensão.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-839">Is targeted by a variety of extension methods.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-840">Declarar seu próprio tipo permite que você adicione sua própria funcionalidade específica da estrutura ao construtor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-840">Declaring your own type allows you to add your own framework-specific functionality to the builder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-841">Não há problema em embrulhar um construtor declarado e encaminhar chamadas para ele.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-841">It's ok to wrap a framework-declared builder and forward calls to it.</span></span>

```csharp
app.UseEndpoints(endpoints =>
{
    // Your framework
    endpoints.MapMyFramework(...).RequrireAuthorization()
                                 .WithMyFrameworkFeature(awesome: true);

    endpoints.MapHealthChecks("/healthz");
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-842">**CONSIDERE** escrever <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.EndpointDataSource>o seu próprio .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-842">**CONSIDER** writing your own <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.EndpointDataSource>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-843">`EndpointDataSource`é o primitivo de baixo nível para declarar e atualizar uma coleção de pontos finais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-843">`EndpointDataSource` is the low-level primitive for declaring and updating a collection of endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-844">`EndpointDataSource`é uma Poderosa API usada por controladores e páginas de barbear.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-844">`EndpointDataSource` is a powerful API used by controllers and Razor Pages.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-845">Os testes de roteamento têm um [exemplo básico](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/Http/Routing/test/testassets/RoutingSandbox/Framework/FrameworkEndpointDataSource.cs#L17) de uma fonte de dados não atualizada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-845">The routing tests have a [basic example](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/Http/Routing/test/testassets/RoutingSandbox/Framework/FrameworkEndpointDataSource.cs#L17) of a non-updating data source.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-846">**NÃO** tente registrar `EndpointDataSource` um por padrão.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-846">**DO NOT** attempt to register an `EndpointDataSource` by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-847">Exija que os usuários <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>registrem sua estrutura em .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-847">Require users to register your framework in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-848">A filosofia do roteamento é que nada `UseEndpoints` está incluído por padrão, e esse é o lugar para registrar pontos finais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-848">The philosophy of routing is that nothing is included by default, and that `UseEndpoints` is the place to register endpoints.</span></span>

### <a name="creating-routing-integrated-middleware"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-849">Criando middleware integrado de roteamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-849">Creating routing-integrated middleware</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-850">**CONSIDERE** definir os tipos de metadados como uma interface.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-850">**CONSIDER** defining metadata types as an interface.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-851">**O DO** torna possível o uso de tipos de metadados como um atributo em classes e métodos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-851">**DO** make it possible to use metadata types as an attribute on classes and methods.</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/ICoolMetadata.cs?name=snippet2)]

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-852">Frameworks como controladores e páginas de barbear suportam a aplicação de atributos de metadados a tipos e métodos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-852">Frameworks like controllers and Razor Pages support applying metadata attributes to types and methods.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-853">Se você declarar tipos de metadados:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-853">If you declare metadata types:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-854">Torná-los acessíveis como [atributos.](/dotnet/csharp/programming-guide/concepts/attributes/)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-854">Make them accessible as [attributes](/dotnet/csharp/programming-guide/concepts/attributes/).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-855">A maioria dos usuários está familiarizada com a aplicação de atributos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-855">Most users are familiar with applying attributes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-856">Declarar um tipo de metadados como interface adiciona outra camada de flexibilidade:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-856">Declaring a metadata type as an interface adds another layer of flexibility:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-857">Interfaces são compostas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-857">Interfaces are composable.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-858">Os desenvolvedores podem declarar seus próprios tipos que combinam várias políticas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-858">Developers can declare their own types that combine multiple policies.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-859">**Do** torna possível substituir metadados, como mostrado no exemplo a seguir:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-859">**DO** make it possible to override metadata, as shown in the following example:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/ICoolMetadata.cs?name=snippet)]

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-860">A melhor maneira de seguir essas diretrizes é evitar a definição de **metadados de marcadores:**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-860">The best way to follow these guidelines is to avoid defining **marker metadata**:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-861">Não basta procurar a presença de um tipo de metadados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-861">Don't just look for the presence of a metadata type.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-862">Defina uma propriedade nos metadados e verifique a propriedade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-862">Define a property on the metadata and check the property.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-863">A coleta de metadados é ordenada e suporta a substituição por prioridade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-863">The metadata collection is ordered and supports overriding by priority.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-864">No caso dos controladores, os metadados sobre o método de ação são mais específicos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-864">In the case of controllers, metadata on the action method is most specific.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-865">**FAÇA** middleware útil com e sem roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-865">**DO** make middleware useful with and without routing.</span></span>

```csharp
app.UseRouting();

app.UseAuthorization(new AuthorizationPolicy() { ... });

app.UseEndpoints(endpoints =>
{
    // Your framework
    endpoints.MapMyFramework(...).RequrireAuthorization();
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-866">Como exemplo desta diretriz, considere `UseAuthorization` o middleware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-866">As an example of this guideline, consider the `UseAuthorization` middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-867">O middleware de autorização permite que você passe em uma política de recuo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-867">The authorization middleware allows you to pass in a fallback policy.</span></span> <!-- shown where?  (shown here) --> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-868">A política de recuo, se especificada, aplica-se a ambos:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-868">The fallback policy, if specified, applies to both:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-869">Endpoints sem uma política especificada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-869">Endpoints without a specified policy.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-870">Pedidos que não correspondem a um ponto final.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-870">Requests that don't match an endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-871">Isso torna o middleware de autorização útil fora do contexto de roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-871">This makes the authorization middleware useful outside of the context of routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-872">O middleware de autorização pode ser usado para programação tradicional de middleware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-872">The authorization middleware can be used for traditional middleware programming.</span></span>

[!INCLUDE[](~/includes/dbg-route.md)]

::: moniker-end

::: moniker range="= aspnetcore-2.2"

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-873">O roteamento é responsável por mapear URIs de solicitação para endpoints e despachar solicitações recebidas para esses pontos finais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-873">Routing is responsible for mapping request URIs to endpoints and dispatching incoming requests to those endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-874">As rotas são definidas no aplicativo e configuradas quando o aplicativo é iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-874">Routes are defined in the app and configured when the app starts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-875">Uma rota pode opcionalmente extrair os valores da URL contida na solicitação e esses valores podem então ser usados para o processamento da solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-875">A route can optionally extract values from the URL contained in the request, and these values can then be used for request processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-876">Usando informações de rota do aplicativo, o roteamento também é capaz de gerar URLs que mapeiam para pontos finais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-876">Using route information from the app, routing is also able to generate URLs that map to endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-877">Para usar os últimos cenários de roteamento no ASP.NET Core 2.2, especifique a [versão de compatibilidade](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) com o registro de serviços MVC em `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-877">To use the latest routing scenarios in ASP.NET Core 2.2, specify the [compatibility version](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) to the MVC services registration in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddMvc()
    .SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_2);
```

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-878">A opção <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.MvcOptions.EnableEndpointRouting> determina se o roteamento deve usar internamente a lógica baseada em ponto de extremidade ou a lógica baseada em <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> do ASP.NET Core 2.1 ou anterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-878">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.MvcOptions.EnableEndpointRouting> option determines if routing should internally use endpoint-based logic or the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>-based logic of ASP.NET Core 2.1 or earlier.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-879">Quando a versão de compatibilidade é definida como 2.2 ou posterior, o valor padrão é `true`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-879">When the compatibility version is set to 2.2 or later, the default value is `true`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-880">Defina o valor como `false` para usar a lógica de roteamento anterior:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-880">Set the value to `false` to use the prior routing logic:</span></span>

```csharp
// Use the routing logic of ASP.NET Core 2.1 or earlier:
services.AddMvc(options => options.EnableEndpointRouting = false)
    .SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_2);
```

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-881">Para obter mais informações sobre o roteamento baseado em <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>, confira a [versão do ASP.NET Core 2.1 deste tópico](/aspnet/core/fundamentals/routing?view=aspnetcore-2.1).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-881">For more information on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>-based routing, see the [ASP.NET Core 2.1 version of this topic](/aspnet/core/fundamentals/routing?view=aspnetcore-2.1).</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-882">Este documento aborda o roteamento de nível inferior do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-882">This document covers low-level ASP.NET Core routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-883">Para obter informações sobre o roteamento do ASP.NET Core MVC, confira <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-883">For information on ASP.NET Core MVC routing, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-884">Para obter informações sobre convenções de roteamento no Razor Pages, confira <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-884">For information on routing conventions in Razor Pages, see <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>
