<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1092">Os métodos `Map[Verb]` usam restrições para limitar a rota ao Verbo HTTP no nome do método.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1092">The `Map[Verb]` methods use constraints to limit the route to the HTTP Verb in the method name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1093">Por exemplo, veja <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> e <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1093">For example, see <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span></span>

## <a name="route-template-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-1094">Referência de modelo de rota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1094">Route template reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1095">Os tokens entre chaves (`{ ... }`) definem os *parâmetros de rota* que serão associados se a rota for correspondida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1095">Tokens within curly braces (`{ ... }`) define *route parameters* that are bound if the route is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1096">Você pode definir mais de um parâmetro de rota em um segmento de rota, mas eles precisam ser separados por um valor literal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1096">You can define more than one route parameter in a route segment, but they must be separated by a literal value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1097">Por exemplo, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` não é uma rota válida, já que não há nenhum valor literal entre `{controller}` e `{action}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1097">For example, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` isn't a valid route, since there's no literal value between `{controller}` and `{action}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1098">Esses parâmetros de rota precisam ter um nome e podem ter atributos adicionais especificados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1098">These route parameters must have a name and may have additional attributes specified.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1099">Um texto literal diferente dos parâmetros de rota (por exemplo, `{id}`) e do separador de caminho `/` precisa corresponder ao texto na URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1099">Literal text other than route parameters (for example, `{id}`) and the path separator `/` must match the text in the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1100">A correspondência de texto não diferencia maiúsculas de minúsculas e se baseia na representação decodificada do caminho de URLs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1100">Text matching is case-insensitive and based on the decoded representation of the URLs path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1101">Para encontrar a correspondência de um delimitador de parâmetro de rota literal (`{` ou `}`), faça o escape do delimitador repetindo o caractere (`{{` ou `}}`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1101">To match a literal route parameter delimiter (`{` or `}`), escape the delimiter by repeating the character (`{{` or `}}`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1102">Padrões de URL que tentam capturar um nome de arquivo com uma extensão de arquivo opcional apresentam considerações adicionais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1102">URL patterns that attempt to capture a file name with an optional file extension have additional considerations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1103">Por exemplo, considere o modelo `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1103">For example, consider the template `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1104">Quando existem valores para `filename` e `ext`, ambos os valores são populados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1104">When values for both `filename` and `ext` exist, both values are populated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1105">Se apenas existir um valor para `filename` na URL, a rota encontrará uma correspondência, pois o ponto à direita (`.`) é opcional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1105">If only a value for `filename` exists in the URL, the route matches because the trailing period (`.`) is  optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1106">As URLs a seguir correspondem a essa rota:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1106">The following URLs match this route:</span></span>

* `/files/myFile.txt`
* `/files/myFile`

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1107">Você pode usar um asterisco (`*`) ou um asterisco duplo (`**`) como um prefixo para um parâmetro de rota para associá-lo ao restante do URI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1107">You can use an asterisk (`*`) or double asterisk (`**`) as a prefix to a route parameter to bind to the rest of the URI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1108">Eles são chamados de parâmetros *catch-all*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1108">These are called a *catch-all* parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1109">Por exemplo, `blog/{**slug}` corresponde a qualquer URI que começa com `/blog` e tem qualquer valor depois dele, que é atribuído ao valor de rota `slug`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1109">For example, `blog/{**slug}` matches any URI that starts with `/blog` and has any value following it, which is assigned to the `slug` route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1110">Os parâmetros catch-all também podem corresponder à cadeia de caracteres vazia.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1110">Catch-all parameters can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1111">O parâmetro catch-all faz o escape dos caracteres corretos quando a rota é usada para gerar uma URL, incluindo os caracteres separadores de caminho (`/`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1111">The catch-all parameter escapes the appropriate characters when the route is used to generate a URL, including path separator (`/`) characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1112">Por exemplo, a rota `foo/{*path}` com valores de rota `{ path = "my/path" }` gera `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1112">For example, the route `foo/{*path}` with route values `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1113">Observe o escape da barra invertida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1113">Note the escaped forward slash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1114">Para fazer a viagem de ida e volta dos caracteres separadores de caminho, use o prefixo do parâmetro da rota `**`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1114">To round-trip path separator characters, use the `**` route parameter prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1115">A rota `foo/{**path}` com `{ path = "my/path" }` gera `foo/my/path`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1115">The route `foo/{**path}` with `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my/path`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1116">Os parâmetros de rota podem ter *valores padrão*, designados pela especificação do valor padrão após o nome do parâmetro separado por um sinal de igual (`=`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1116">Route parameters may have *default values* designated by specifying the default value after the parameter name separated by an equals sign (`=`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1117">Por exemplo, `{controller=Home}` define `Home` como o valor padrão de `controller`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1117">For example, `{controller=Home}` defines `Home` as the default value for `controller`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1118">O valor padrão é usado se nenhum valor está presente na URL para o parâmetro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1118">The default value is used if no value is present in the URL for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1119">Os parâmetros de rota se tornam opcionais com o acréscimo de um ponto de interrogação (`?`) ao final do nome do parâmetro, como em `id?`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1119">Route parameters are made optional by appending a question mark (`?`) to the end of the parameter name, as in `id?`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1120">A diferença entre valores opcionais e parâmetros de rota padrão é que um parâmetro de rota com um valor padrão sempre produz um valor – um parâmetro opcional tem um valor somente quando um valor é fornecido pela URL de solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1120">The difference between optional values and default route parameters is that a route parameter with a default value always produces a value&mdash;an optional parameter has a value only when a value is provided by the request URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1121">Os parâmetros de rota podem ter restrições que precisam corresponder ao valor de rota associado da URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1121">Route parameters may have constraints that must match the route value bound from the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1122">A adição de dois-pontos (`:`) e do nome da restrição após o nome do parâmetro de rota especifica uma *restrição embutida* em um parâmetro de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1122">Adding a colon (`:`) and constraint name after the route parameter name specifies an *inline constraint* on a route parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1123">Se a restrição exigir argumentos, eles ficarão entre parênteses (`(...)`) após o nome da restrição.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1123">If the constraint requires arguments, they're enclosed in parentheses (`(...)`) after the constraint name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1124">Várias restrições embutidas podem ser especificadas por meio do acréscimo de outros dois-pontos (`:`) e do nome da restrição.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1124">Multiple inline constraints can be specified by appending another colon (`:`) and constraint name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1125">O nome da restrição e os argumentos são passados para o serviço <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> para criar uma instância de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> a ser usada no processamento de URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1125">The constraint name and arguments are passed to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> service to create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> to use in URL processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1126">Por exemplo, o modelo de rota `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` especifica uma restrição `minlength` com o argumento `10`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1126">For example, the route template `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifies a `minlength` constraint with the argument `10`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1127">Para obter mais informações sobre as restrições de rota e uma lista das restrições fornecidas pela estrutura, confira a seção [Referência de restrição de rota](#route-constraint-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1127">For more information on route constraints and a list of the constraints provided by the framework, see the [Route constraint reference](#route-constraint-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1128">Os parâmetros de rota também podem ter transformadores de parâmetro, que transformam o valor de um parâmetro ao gerar links e fazer a correspondência de ações e páginas com URLs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1128">Route parameters may also have parameter transformers, which transform a parameter's value when generating links and matching actions and pages to URLs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1129">Assim como as restrições, os transformadores de parâmetro podem ser adicionados embutidos a um parâmetro de rota colocando dois-pontos (`:`) e o nome do transformador após o nome do parâmetro de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1129">Like constraints, parameter transformers can be added inline to a route parameter by adding a colon (`:`) and transformer name after the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1130">Por exemplo, o modelo de rota `blog/{article:slugify}` especifica um transformador `slugify`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1130">For example, the route template `blog/{article:slugify}` specifies a `slugify` transformer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1131">Para obter mais informações sobre transformadores de parâmetro, confira a seção [Referência de transformador de parâmetro](#parameter-transformer-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1131">For more information on parameter transformers, see the [Parameter transformer reference](#parameter-transformer-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1132">A tabela a seguir demonstra modelos de rota de exemplo e seu comportamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1132">The following table demonstrates example route templates and their behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1133">Modelo de rota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1133">Route Template</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1134">URI de correspondência de exemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1134">Example Matching URI</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1135">O URI de solicitação&hellip;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1135">The request URI&hellip;</span></span>                                                    |
| ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `hello`                                  | `/hello`                | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1136">Somente corresponde ao caminho único `/hello`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1136">Only matches the single path `/hello`.</span></span>                                     |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1137">Faz a correspondência e define `Page` como `Home`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1137">Matches and sets `Page` to `Home`.</span></span>                                         |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/Contact`              | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1138">Faz a correspondência e define `Page` como `Contact`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1138">Matches and sets `Page` to `Contact`.</span></span>                                      |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/List`        | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1139">É mapeado para o controlador `Products` e a ação `List`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1139">Maps to the `Products` controller and `List` action.</span></span>                       |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/Details/123` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1140">É mapeado para o controlador `Products` e a ação `Details` (`id` definido como 123).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1140">Maps to the `Products` controller and  `Details` action (`id` set to 123).</span></span> |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1141">É mapeado para o controlador `Home` e o método `Index` (`id` é ignorado).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1141">Maps to the `Home` controller and `Index` method (`id` is ignored).</span></span>        |

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1142">Em geral, o uso de um modelo é a abordagem mais simples para o roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1142">Using a template is generally the simplest approach to routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1143">Restrições e padrões também podem ser especificados fora do modelo de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1143">Constraints and defaults can also be specified outside the route template.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1144">Habilite o [Log](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) para ver como as implementações de roteamento internas, como <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, correspondem às solicitações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1144">Enable [Logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) to see how the built-in routing implementations, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, match requests.</span></span>

## <a name="reserved-routing-names"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-1145">Nomes reservados de roteamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1145">Reserved routing names</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1146">As seguintes palavras-chave são nomes reservados e não podem ser usadas como nomes de rota ou parâmetros:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1146">The following keywords are reserved names and can't be used as route names or parameters:</span></span>

* `action`
* `area`
* `controller`
* `handler`
* `page`

## <a name="route-constraint-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-1147">Referência de restrição de rota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1147">Route constraint reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1148">As restrições de rota são executadas quando ocorre uma correspondência com a URL de entrada e é criado um token do caminho da URL em valores de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1148">Route constraints execute when a match has occurred to the incoming URL and the URL path is tokenized into route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1149">Em geral, as restrições da rota inspecionam o valor de rota associado por meio do modelo de rota e tomam uma decisão do tipo "sim/não" sobre se o valor é aceitável ou não.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1149">Route constraints generally inspect the route value associated via the route template and make a yes/no decision about whether or not the value is acceptable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1150">Algumas restrições da rota usam dados fora do valor de rota para considerar se a solicitação pode ser encaminhada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1150">Some route constraints use data outside the route value to consider whether the request can be routed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1151">Por exemplo, a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> pode aceitar ou rejeitar uma solicitação de acordo com o verbo HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1151">For example, the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> can accept or reject a request based on its HTTP verb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1152">As restrições são usadas em solicitações de roteamento e na geração de link.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1152">Constraints are used in routing requests and link generation.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1153">Não use restrições para a **validação de entrada**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1153">Don't use constraints for **input validation**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1154">Se as restrições forem usadas para a **validação de entrada**, uma entrada inválida resultará em uma resposta *404 – Não Encontrado*, em vez de *400 – Solicitação Inválida* com uma mensagem de erro apropriada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1154">If constraints are used for **input validation**, invalid input results in a *404 - Not Found* response instead of a *400 - Bad Request* with an appropriate error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1155">As restrições de rota são usadas para **desfazer a ambiguidade** entre rotas semelhantes, não para validar as entradas de uma rota específica.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1155">Route constraints are used to **disambiguate** similar routes, not to validate the inputs for a particular route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1156">A tabela a seguir demonstra restrições de rota de exemplo e seu comportamento esperado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1156">The following table demonstrates example route constraints and their expected behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1157">restrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1157">constraint</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1158">Exemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1158">Example</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1159">Correspondências de exemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1159">Example Matches</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1160">Observações</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1160">Notes</span></span> |
| ---------- | ------- | --------------- | ----- |
| `int` | `{id:int}` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1161">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1161">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1162">Combina com qualquer inteiro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1162">Matches any integer.</span></span> |
| `bool` | `{active:bool}` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1163">`true`, `FALSE`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1163">`true`, `FALSE`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1164">Fósforos `true` ou falsos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1164">Matches `true` or \`false.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1165">Caso insensível.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1165">Case-insensitive.</span></span> |
| `datetime` | `{dob:datetime}` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1166">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1166">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1167">Corresponde a `DateTime` um valor válido na cultura invariante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1167">Matches a valid `DateTime` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1168">Veja o aviso anterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1168">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `decimal` | `{price:decimal}` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1169">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1169">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1170">Corresponde a `decimal` um valor válido na cultura invariante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1170">Matches a valid `decimal` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1171">Veja o aviso anterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1171">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `double` | `{weight:double}` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1172">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1172">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1173">Corresponde a `double` um valor válido na cultura invariante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1173">Matches a valid `double` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1174">Veja o aviso anterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1174">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `float` | `{weight:float}` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1175">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1175">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1176">Corresponde a `float` um valor válido na cultura invariante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1176">Matches a valid `float` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1177">Veja o aviso anterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1177">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `guid` | `{id:guid}` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1178">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1178">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1179">Corresponde a `Guid` um valor válido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1179">Matches a valid `Guid` value.</span></span> |
| `long` | `{ticks:long}` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1180">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1180">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1181">Corresponde a `long` um valor válido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1181">Matches a valid `long` value.</span></span> |
| `minlength(value)` | `{username:minlength(4)}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1182">String deve ser de pelo menos 4 caracteres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1182">String must be at least 4 characters.</span></span> |
| `maxlength(value)` | `{filename:maxlength(8)}` | `MyFile` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1183">String tem no máximo 8 caracteres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1183">String has maximum of 8 characters.</span></span> |
| `length(length)` | `{filename:length(12)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1184">A corda deve ter exatamente 12 caracteres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1184">String must be exactly 12 characters long.</span></span> |
| `length(min,max)` | `{filename:length(8,16)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1185">A corda deve ter pelo menos 8 e tem no máximo 16 caracteres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1185">String must be at least 8 and has maximum of 16 characters.</span></span> |
| `min(value)` | `{age:min(18)}` | `19` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1186">O valor inteiro deve ser de pelo menos 18.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1186">Integer value must be at least 18.</span></span> |
| `max(value)` | `{age:max(120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1187">Valor total de 120.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1187">Integer value maximum of 120.</span></span> |
| `range(min,max)` | `{age:range(18,120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1188">O valor inteiro deve ser de no mínimo 18 e máximo de 120.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1188">Integer value must be at least 18 and maximum of 120.</span></span> |
| `alpha` | `{name:alpha}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1189">String deve consistir de um `a` - `z`ou mais caracteres alfabéticos .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1189">String must consist of one or more alphabetical characters `a`-`z`.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1190">Caso insensível.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1190">Case-insensitive.</span></span> |
| `regex(expression)` | `{ssn:regex(^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$)}` | `123-45-6789` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1191">A corda deve corresponder à expressão regular.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1191">String must match the regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1192">Veja dicas sobre como definir uma expressão regular.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1192">See tips about defining a regular expression.</span></span> |
| `required` | `{name:required}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1193">Usado para impor que um valor não parâmetro está presente durante a geração de URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1193">Used to enforce that a non-parameter value is present during URL generation.</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1194">Várias restrições delimitadas por vírgula podem ser aplicadas a um único parâmetro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1194">Multiple, colon-delimited constraints can be applied to a single parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1195">Por exemplo, a restrição a seguir restringe um parâmetro para um valor inteiro de 1 ou maior:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1195">For example, the following constraint restricts a parameter to an integer value of 1 or greater:</span></span>

```csharp
[Route("users/{id:int:min(1)}")]
public User GetUserById(int id) { }
```

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1196">As restrições de rota que verificam a URL e são convertidas em um tipo CLR (como `int` ou `DateTime`) sempre usam a cultura invariável.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1196">Route constraints that verify the URL and are converted to a CLR type (such as `int` or `DateTime`) always use the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1197">Essas restrições consideram que a URL não é localizável.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1197">These constraints assume that the URL is non-localizable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1198">As restrições de rota fornecidas pela estrutura não modificam os valores armazenados nos valores de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1198">The framework-provided route constraints don't modify the values stored in route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1199">Todos os valores de rota analisados com base na URL são armazenados como cadeias de caracteres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1199">All route values parsed from the URL are stored as strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1200">Por exemplo, a restrição `float` tenta converter o valor de rota em um float, mas o valor convertido é usado somente para verificar se ele pode ser convertido em um float.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1200">For example, the `float` constraint attempts to convert the route value to a float, but the converted value is used only to verify it can be converted to a float.</span></span>

## <a name="regular-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-1201">Expressões regulares</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1201">Regular expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1202">A estrutura do ASP.NET Core adiciona `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` ao construtor de expressão regular.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1202">The ASP.NET Core framework adds `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` to the regular expression constructor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1203">Confira <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> para obter uma descrição desses membros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1203">See <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> for a description of these members.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1204">Expressões regulares usam delimitadores e tokens semelhantes aos usados pelo roteamento e pela linguagem C#.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1204">Regular expressions use delimiters and tokens similar to those used by routing and the C# language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1205">Os tokens de expressão regular precisam ter escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1205">Regular expression tokens must be escaped.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1206">Para usar a `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` expressão regular no roteamento:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1206">To use the regular expression `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` in routing:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1207">A expressão deve ter `\` os caracteres de barra invertida única fornecidos na seqüência como caracteres de barra invertida `\\` dupla no código-fonte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1207">The expression must have the single backslash `\` characters provided in the string as double backslash `\\` characters in the source code.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1208">A expressão regular `\\` deve-nos `\` para escapar do personagem de fuga de cordas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1208">The regular expression must us `\\` in order to escape the `\` string escape character.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1209">A expressão regular não `\\` requer ao usar [literais de cordas verbatim](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1209">The regular expression doesn't require `\\` when using [verbatim string literals](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1210">Para `{`escapar dos caracteres delimitadores do parâmetro de roteamento, `}` `[`o `]`dobro dos caracteres na expressão, `{{` `}`mas `[[`. `]]`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1210">To escape routing parameter delimiter characters `{`, `}`, `[`, `]`, double the characters in the expression `{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1211">A tabela a seguir mostra uma expressão regular e a versão fugitiva:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1211">The following table shows a regular expression and the escaped version:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1212">Expressão regular</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1212">Regular Expression</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1213">Expressão regular com escape</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1213">Escaped Regular Expression</span></span>     |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` | `^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$` |
| `^[a-z]{2}$`          | `^[[a-z]]{{2}}$`               |

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1214">Expressões regulares usadas no roteamento `^` geralmente começam com o caractere caret e correspondem à posição inicial da string.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1214">Regular expressions used in routing often start with the caret `^` character and match starting position of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1215">As expressões geralmente terminam `$` com o caractere do sinal de dólar e a extremidade da seqüência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1215">The expressions often end with the dollar sign `$` character and match end of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1216">Os caracteres `^` e `$` garantem que a expressão regular corresponde a todo o valor do parâmetro de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1216">The `^` and `$` characters ensure that the regular expression match the entire route parameter value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1217">Sem os caracteres `^` e `$`, a expressão regular corresponde a qualquer subcadeia de caracteres na cadeia de caracteres, o que geralmente não é o desejado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1217">Without the `^` and `$` characters, the regular expression match any substring within the string, which is often undesirable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1218">A tabela a seguir fornece exemplos e explica por que eles encontram ou não uma correspondência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1218">The following table provides examples and explains why they match or fail to match.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1219">Expression</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1219">Expression</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1220">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1220">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1221">Corresponder a</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1221">Match</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1222">Comentário</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1222">Comment</span></span>               |
| ------------ | --------- | :---: |  -------------------- |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1223">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1223">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1224">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1224">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1225">A subcadeia de caracteres corresponde</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1225">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1226">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1226">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1227">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1227">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1228">A subcadeia de caracteres corresponde</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1228">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1229">mz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1229">mz</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1230">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1230">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1231">Corresponde à expressão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1231">Matches expression</span></span>    |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1232">MZ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1232">MZ</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1233">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1233">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1234">Não diferencia maiúsculas de minúsculas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1234">Not case sensitive</span></span>    |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1235">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1235">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1236">Não</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1236">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1237">Confira `^` e `$` acima</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1237">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1238">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1238">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1239">Não</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1239">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1240">Confira `^` e `$` acima</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1240">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1241">Para saber mais sobre a sintaxe de expressões regulares, confira [Expressões regulares do .NET Framework](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1241">For more information on regular expression syntax, see [.NET Framework Regular Expressions](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1242">Para restringir um parâmetro a um conjunto conhecido de valores possíveis, use uma expressão regular.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1242">To constrain a parameter to a known set of possible values, use a regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1243">Por exemplo, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` apenas corresponde o valor da rota `action` a `list`, `get` ou `create`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1243">For example, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` only matches the `action` route value to `list`, `get`, or `create`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1244">Se passada para o dicionário de restrições, a cadeia de caracteres `^(list|get|create)$` é equivalente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1244">If passed into the constraints dictionary, the string `^(list|get|create)$` is equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1245">As restrições passadas para o dicionário de restrições (não embutidas em um modelo) que não correspondem a uma das restrições conhecidas também são tratadas como expressões regulares.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1245">Constraints that are passed in the constraints dictionary (not inline within a template) that don't match one of the known constraints are also treated as regular expressions.</span></span>

## <a name="custom-route-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-1246">Restrições de rota personalizadas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1246">Custom route constraints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1247">Além das restrições de rota internas, é possível criar restrições de rota personalizadas com a implementação da interface do <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1247">In addition to the built-in route constraints, custom route constraints can be created by implementing the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1248">A interface do <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> contém um único método, `Match`, que retorna `true` quando a restrição é satisfeita. Caso contrário, retorna `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1248">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface contains a single method, `Match`, which returns `true` if the constraint is satisfied and `false` otherwise.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1249">Para usar uma <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> personalizada, o tipo de restrição de rota deve ser registrado com o <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> do aplicativo, no contêiner de serviço do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1249">To use a custom <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>, the route constraint type must be registered with the app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in the app's service container.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1250">O <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> é um dicionário que mapeia as chaves de restrição de rota para implementações de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> que validam essas restrições.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1250">A <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> is a dictionary that maps route constraint keys to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> implementations that validate those constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1251">É possível atualizar o <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> do aplicativo no `Startup.ConfigureServices` como parte de uma chamada [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) ou configurando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> diretamente com `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1251">An app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> can be updated in `Startup.ConfigureServices` either as part of a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) call or by configuring <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directly with `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1252">Por exemplo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1252">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    options.ConstraintMap.Add("customName", typeof(MyCustomConstraint));
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1253">a restrição pode então ser aplicada às rotas da maneira usual, usando o nome especificado ao registrar o tipo de restrição.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1253">The constraint can then be applied to routes in the usual manner, using the name specified when registering the constraint type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1254">Por exemplo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1254">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
[HttpGet("{id:customName}")]
public ActionResult<string> Get(string id)
```

## <a name="parameter-transformer-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-1255">Referência de parâmetro de transformador</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1255">Parameter transformer reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1256">Transformadores de parâmetro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1256">Parameter transformers:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1257">Executar ao gerar um link para um <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1257">Execute when generating a link for a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1258">Implementar `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IOutboundParameterTransformer`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1258">Implement `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IOutboundParameterTransformer`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1259">São configurados usando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1259">Are configured using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1260">Usam o valor de rota do parâmetro e o transformam em um novo valor de cadeia de caracteres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1260">Take the parameter's route value and transform it to a new string value.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1261">Resultam no uso do valor transformado no link gerado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1261">Result in using the transformed value in the generated link.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1262">Por exemplo, um transformador de parâmetro `slugify` personalizado em padrão de rota `blog\{article:slugify}` com `Url.Action(new { article = "MyTestArticle" })` gera `blog\my-test-article`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1262">For example, a custom `slugify` parameter transformer in route pattern `blog\{article:slugify}` with `Url.Action(new { article = "MyTestArticle" })` generates `blog\my-test-article`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1263">Para usar um transformador de parâmetro em um padrão de rota, configure-o primeiro usando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> em `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1263">To use a parameter transformer in a route pattern, configure it first using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    // Replace the type and the name used to refer to it with your own
    // IOutboundParameterTransformer implementation
    options.ConstraintMap["slugify"] = typeof(SlugifyParameterTransformer);
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1264">Os transformadores de parâmetro são usados pela estrutura para transformar o URI no qual um ponto de extremidade é resolvido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1264">Parameter transformers are used by the framework to transform the URI where an endpoint resolves.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1265">Por exemplo, o ASP.NET Core MVC usa os transformadores de parâmetro para transformar o valor de rota usado para corresponder a um `area`, `controller`, `action` e `page`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1265">For example, ASP.NET Core MVC uses parameter transformers to transform the route value used to match an `area`, `controller`, `action`, and `page`.</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller:slugify=Home}/{action:slugify=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1266">Com a rota anterior, a ação `SubscriptionManagementController.GetAll` é combinada com o URI `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1266">With the preceding route, the action `SubscriptionManagementController.GetAll` is matched with the URI `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1267">Um transformador de parâmetro não altera os valores de rota usados para gerar um link.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1267">A parameter transformer doesn't change the route values used to generate a link.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1268">Por exemplo, `Url.Action("GetAll", "SubscriptionManagement")` gera `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1268">For example, `Url.Action("GetAll", "SubscriptionManagement")` outputs `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1269">ASP.NET Core fornece convenções de API para usar transformadores de parâmetro com as rotas geradas:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1269">ASP.NET Core provides API conventions for using a parameter transformers with generated routes:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1270">ASP.NET Core MVC tem a convenção de API `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.RouteTokenTransformerConvention`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1270">ASP.NET Core MVC has the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.RouteTokenTransformerConvention` API convention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1271">Essa convenção aplica um transformador de parâmetro especificado a todas as rotas de atributo no aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1271">This convention applies a specified parameter transformer to all attribute routes in the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1272">O transformador de parâmetro transforma os tokens de rota do atributo conforme elas são substituídas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1272">The parameter transformer transforms attribute route tokens as they are replaced.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1273">Para obter mais informações, confira [Usar um transformador de parâmetro para personalizar a substituição de token](/aspnet/core/mvc/controllers/routing#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-token-replacement).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1273">For more information, see [Use a parameter transformer to customize token replacement](/aspnet/core/mvc/controllers/routing#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-token-replacement).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1274">O Razor Pages tem a convenção de API `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.PageRouteTransformerConvention`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1274">Razor Pages has the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.PageRouteTransformerConvention` API convention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1275">Essa convenção aplica um transformador de parâmetro especificado a todas as Razor Pages descobertas automaticamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1275">This convention applies a specified parameter transformer to all automatically discovered Razor Pages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1276">O transformador de parâmetro transforma os segmentos de nome de arquivo e pasta de rotas do Razor Pages.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1276">The parameter transformer transforms the folder and file name segments of Razor Pages routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1277">Para obter mais informações, confira [Usar um transformador de parâmetros para personalizar rotas de página](/aspnet/core/razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-page-routes).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1277">For more information, see [Use a parameter transformer to customize page routes](/aspnet/core/razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-page-routes).</span></span>

## <a name="url-generation-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-1278">Referência de geração de URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1278">URL generation reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1279">O exemplo a seguir mostra como gerar um link para uma rota com base em um dicionário de valores de rota e em um <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1279">The following example shows how to generate a link to a route given a dictionary of route values and a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_Dictionary)]

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1280">O <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> gerado no final do exemplo anterior é `/package/create/123`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1280">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generated at the end of the preceding sample is `/package/create/123`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1281">O dicionário fornece os valores de rota `operation` e `id` do modelo "Rastrear rota do pacote", `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1281">The dictionary supplies the `operation` and `id` route values of the "Track Package Route" template, `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1282">Para obter detalhes, consulte o código de exemplo na seção [Usar o middleware de roteamento](#use-routing-middleware) ou no [aplicativo de exemplo](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1282">For details, see the sample code in the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section or the [sample app](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1283">O segundo parâmetro para o construtor <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> é uma coleção de *valores de ambiente*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1283">The second parameter to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> constructor is a collection of *ambient values*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1284">Os valores de ambiente são convenientes de serem usados porque limitam o número de valores que um desenvolvedor precisa especificar em um contexto de solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1284">Ambient values are convenient to use because they limit the number of values a developer must specify within a request context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1285">Os valores de rota atuais da solicitação atual são considerados valores de ambiente para a geração de link.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1285">The current route values of the current request are considered ambient values for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1286">Na ação `About` de um aplicativo ASP.NET Core MVC do `HomeController`, não é necessário especificar o valor de rota do controlador a ser vinculado à ação `Index` – o valor de ambiente `Home` é usado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1286">In an ASP.NET Core MVC app's `About` action of the `HomeController`, you don't need to specify the controller route value to link to the `Index` action&mdash;the ambient value of `Home` is used.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1287">Os valores de ambiente que não correspondem a um parâmetro são ignorados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1287">Ambient values that don't match a parameter are ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1288">Os valores de ambiente também são ignorados quando um valor fornecido explicitamente substitui o valor de ambiente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1288">Ambient values are also ignored when an explicitly provided value overrides the ambient value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1289">A correspondência ocorre da esquerda para a direita na URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1289">Matching occurs from left to right in the URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1290">Valores fornecidos explicitamente, mas que não correspondem a um segmento da rota, são adicionados à cadeia de consulta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1290">Values explicitly provided but that don't match a segment of the route are added to the query string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1291">A tabela a seguir mostra o resultado do uso do modelo de rota `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1291">The following table shows the result when using the route template `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1292">Valores de ambiente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1292">Ambient Values</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1293">Valores explícitos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1293">Explicit Values</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1294">Result</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1294">Result</span></span>                  |
| ---------------------------------- | -------------------------------------- | ----------------------- |
| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1295">controlador = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1295">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1296">ação = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1296">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1297">controlador = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1297">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1298">controlador = "Order", ação = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1298">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span></span> | `/Order/About`          |
| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1299">controlador = "Home", cor = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1299">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1300">ação = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1300">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1301">controlador = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1301">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1302">ação = "About", cor = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1302">action = "About", color = "Red"</span></span>        | `/Home/About?color=Red` |

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1303">Se uma rota tem um valor padrão que não corresponde a um parâmetro e esse valor é fornecido de forma explícita, ele precisa corresponder ao valor padrão:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1303">If a route has a default value that doesn't correspond to a parameter and that value is explicitly provided, it must match the default value:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute("blog_route", "blog/{*slug}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadPost" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1304">A geração de link somente gera um link para essa rota quando os valores correspondentes de `controller` e `action` são fornecidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1304">Link generation only generates a link for this route when the matching values for `controller` and `action` are provided.</span></span>

## <a name="complex-segments"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-1305">Segmentos complexos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1305">Complex segments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1306">Segmentos complexos (por exemplo, `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) são processados por meio da combinação de literais da direita para a esquerda, de uma maneira diferente de Greedy.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1306">Complex segments (for example `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) are processed by matching up literals from right to left in a non-greedy way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1307">Confira [este código](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) para ver uma explicação detalhada de como os segmentos complexos são combinados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1307">See [this code](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) for a detailed explanation of how complex segments are matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1308">O [exemplo de código](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) não é usado pelo ASP.NET Core, mas fornece uma explicação adequada sobre segmentos complexos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1308">The [code sample](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) is not used by ASP.NET Core, but it provides a good explanation of complex segments.</span></span>

::: moniker range="< aspnetcore-2.2"

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1309">O roteamento é responsável por mapear URIs de solicitação para manipuladores de rotas e expedir as solicitações de entrada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1309">Routing is responsible for mapping request URIs to route handlers and dispatching an incoming requests.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1310">As rotas são definidas no aplicativo e configuradas quando o aplicativo é iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1310">Routes are defined in the app and configured when the app starts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1311">Uma rota pode opcionalmente extrair os valores da URL contida na solicitação e esses valores podem então ser usados para o processamento da solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1311">A route can optionally extract values from the URL contained in the request, and these values can then be used for request processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1312">Usando rotas configuradas no aplicativo, o roteamento pode gerar URLs que são mapeadas para manipuladores de rotas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1312">Using configured routes from the app, routing is able to generate URLs that map to route handlers.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1313">Para usar os últimos cenários de roteamento no ASP.NET Core 2.1, especifique a [versão de compatibilidade](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) com o registro de serviços MVC em `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1313">To use the latest routing scenarios in ASP.NET Core 2.1, specify the [compatibility version](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) to the MVC services registration in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddMvc()
    .SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_1);
```

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1314">Este documento aborda o roteamento de nível inferior do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1314">This document covers low-level ASP.NET Core routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1315">Para obter informações sobre o roteamento do ASP.NET Core MVC, confira <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1315">For information on ASP.NET Core MVC routing, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1316">Para obter informações sobre convenções de roteamento no Razor Pages, confira <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1316">For information on routing conventions in Razor Pages, see <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1317">[Exibir ou baixar código de exemplo](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples) ([como baixar](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1317">[View or download sample code](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples) ([how to download](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span></span>

## <a name="routing-basics"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-1318">Conceitos básicos sobre roteamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1318">Routing basics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1319">A maioria dos aplicativos deve escolher um esquema de roteamento básico e descritivo para que as URLs sejam legíveis e significativas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1319">Most apps should choose a basic and descriptive routing scheme so that URLs are readable and meaningful.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1320">A rota convencional padrão `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1320">The default conventional route `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1321">Dá suporte a um esquema de roteamento básico e descritivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1321">Supports a basic and descriptive routing scheme.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1322">É um ponto de partida útil para aplicativos baseados em interface do usuário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1322">Is a useful starting point for UI-based apps.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1323">Os desenvolvedores geralmente adicionam outras rotas concisas às áreas de alto tráfego de um aplicativo em situações especiais (por exemplo, pontos de extremidade de blog e comércio eletrônico) usando o [roteamento de atributo](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#attribute-routing) ou rotas convencionais dedicadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1323">Developers commonly add additional terse routes to high-traffic areas of an app in specialized situations (for example, blog and ecommerce endpoints) using [attribute routing](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#attribute-routing) or dedicated conventional routes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1324">As APIs da Web devem usar o roteamento de atributo para modelar a funcionalidade do aplicativo como um conjunto de recursos em que as operações são representadas por verbos HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1324">Web APIs should use attribute routing to model the app's functionality as a set of resources where operations are represented by HTTP verbs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1325">Isso significa que muitas operações (por exemplo, GET, POST) no mesmo recurso lógico usarão a mesma URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1325">This means that many operations (for example, GET, POST) on the same logical resource will use the same URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1326">O roteamento de atributo fornece um nível de controle necessário para projetar cuidadosamente o layout de ponto de extremidade público de uma API.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1326">Attribute routing provides a level of control that's needed to carefully design an API's public endpoint layout.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1327">Os aplicativos do Razor Pages usam o roteamento convencional padrão para fornecer recursos nomeados na pasta *Pages* de um aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1327">Razor Pages apps use default conventional routing to serve named resources in the *Pages* folder of an app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1328">Estão disponíveis convenções adicionais que permitem a personalização do comportamento de roteamento do Razor Pages.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1328">Additional conventions are available that allow you to customize Razor Pages routing behavior.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1329">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:razor-pages/index> e <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1329">For more information, see <xref:razor-pages/index> and <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1330">O suporte à geração de URL permite que o aplicativo seja desenvolvido sem hard-coding das URLs para vincular o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1330">URL generation support allows the app to be developed without hard-coding URLs to link the app together.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1331">Esse suporte permite começar com uma configuração de roteamento básica e modificar as rotas, depois que o layout de recurso do aplicativo é determinado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1331">This support allows for starting with a basic routing configuration and modifying the routes after the app's resource layout is determined.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1332">O roteamento utiliza <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> implementações de rotas de:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1332">Routing uses routes implementations of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> to:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1333">Mapear solicitações de entrada para *manipuladores de rotas*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1333">Map incoming requests to *route handlers*.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1334">Gerar as URLs usadas nas respostas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1334">Generate the URLs used in responses.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1335">Por padrão, um aplicativo tem uma única coleção de rotas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1335">By default, an app has a single collection of routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1336">Quando uma solicitação é recebida, as rotas na coleção são processadas na ordem em que existem na coleção.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1336">When a request arrives, the routes in the collection are processed in the order that they exist in the collection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1337">A estrutura tenta corresponder uma URL de solicitação de entrada a uma rota na coleção chamando o método <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> em cada rota da coleção.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1337">The framework attempts to match an incoming request URL to a route in the collection by calling the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> method on each route in the collection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1338">Uma resposta pode usar o roteamento para gerar URLs (por exemplo, para redirecionamento ou links) com base nas informações de rotas e evitar URLs embutidas em código, o que ajuda na facilidade de manutenção.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1338">A response can use routing to generate URLs (for example, for redirection or links) based on route information and thus avoid hard-coded URLs, which helps maintainability.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1339">O sistema de roteamento tem as seguintes características:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1339">The routing system has the following characteristics:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1340">A sintaxe do modelo de rota é usada para definir rotas com os parâmetros de rota com tokens criados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1340">Route template syntax is used to define routes with tokenized route parameters.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1341">A configuração de ponto de extremidade de estilo convencional e de estilo de atributo é permitida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1341">Conventional-style and attribute-style endpoint configuration is permitted.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1342"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> é usado para determinar se um parâmetro de URL contém um valor válido para determinada restrição de ponto de extremidade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1342"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> is used to determine whether a URL parameter contains a valid value for a given endpoint constraint.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1343">Modelos de aplicativo, como MVC/Razor Pages, registram todas as suas rotas, que têm uma implementação previsível de cenários de roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1343">App models, such as MVC/Razor Pages, register all of their routes, which have a predictable implementation of routing scenarios.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1344">Uma resposta pode usar o roteamento para gerar URLs (por exemplo, para redirecionamento ou links) com base nas informações de rotas e evitar URLs embutidas em código, o que ajuda na facilidade de manutenção.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1344">A response can use routing to generate URLs (for example, for redirection or links) based on route information and thus avoid hard-coded URLs, which helps maintainability.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1345">A geração de URL baseia-se em rotas, que dá suporte à extensibilidade arbitrária.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1345">URL generation is based on routes, which support arbitrary extensibility.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1346"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> oferece métodos para criar URLs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1346"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> offers methods to build URLs.</span></span>
<!-- fix [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) -->
<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1347">O roteamento está conectado ao pipeline do [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) pela classe <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RouterMiddleware>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1347">Routing is connected to the [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) pipeline by the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RouterMiddleware> class.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1348">O [ASP.NET Core MVC](xref:mvc/overview) adiciona o roteamento ao pipeline de middleware como parte de sua configuração e manipula o roteamento nos aplicativos do MVC e do Razor Pages.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1348">[ASP.NET Core MVC](xref:mvc/overview) adds routing to the middleware pipeline as part of its configuration and handles routing in MVC and Razor Pages apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1349">Para saber como usar o roteamento como um componente autônomo, confira a seção [Usar o Middleware de Roteamento](#use-routing-middleware).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1349">To learn how to use routing as a standalone component, see the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section.</span></span>

### <a name="url-matching"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-1350">Correspondência de URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1350">URL matching</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1351">Correspondência de URL é o processo pelo qual o roteamento expede uma solicitação de entrada para um *manipulador*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1351">URL matching is the process by which routing dispatches an incoming request to a *handler*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1352">Esse processo se baseia nos dados do caminho da URL, mas pode ser estendido para considerar qualquer dado na solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1352">This process is based on data in the URL path but can be extended to consider any data in the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1353">A capacidade de expedir solicitações para manipuladores separados é fundamental para dimensionar o tamanho e a complexidade de um aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1353">The ability to dispatch requests to separate handlers is key to scaling the size and complexity of an app.</span></span>
