<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1354">As solicitações de entrada entram no <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RouterMiddleware>, que chama o método <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> em cada rota na sequência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1354">Incoming requests enter the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RouterMiddleware>, which calls the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> method on each route in sequence.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1355">A instância <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> escolhe se deseja *manipular* a solicitação definindo o [RouteContext.Handler](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.Handler*) como um <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate> não nulo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1355">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> instance chooses whether to *handle* the request by setting the [RouteContext.Handler](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.Handler*) to a non-null <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1356">Se uma rota definir um manipulador para a solicitação, o processamento de rotas será interrompido e o manipulador será invocado para processar a solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1356">If a route sets a handler for the request, route processing stops, and the handler is invoked to process the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1357">Se nenhum manipulador de rotas é encontrado para processar a solicitação, o middleware transmite a solicitação para o próximo middleware no pipeline de solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1357">If no route handler is found to process the request, the middleware hands the request off to the next middleware in the request pipeline.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1358">A entrada primária para <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> é o [RouteContext.HttpContext](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.HttpContext*) associado à solicitação atual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1358">The primary input to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> is the [RouteContext.HttpContext](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.HttpContext*) associated with the current request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1359">[RouteContext.Handler](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.Handler) e [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData*) são saídas definidas depois que é encontrada uma correspondência de uma rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1359">The [RouteContext.Handler](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.Handler) and [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData*) are outputs set after a route is matched.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1360">Uma correspondência que chama <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> também define as propriedades do [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) com valores apropriados com base no processamento da solicitação executado até o momento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1360">A match that calls <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> also sets the properties of the [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) to appropriate values based on the request processing performed thus far.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1361">[RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values*) é um dicionário de *valores de rota* produzido por meio da rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1361">[RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values*) is a dictionary of *route values* produced from the route.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1362">Esses valores geralmente são determinados pela criação de token da URL e podem ser usados para aceitar a entrada do usuário ou tomar outras decisões de expedição dentro do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1362">These values are usually determined by tokenizing the URL and can be used to accept user input or to make further dispatching decisions inside the app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1363">[RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) é um recipiente de propriedades de dados adicionais relacionados à rota correspondente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1363">[RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) is a property bag of additional data related to the matched route.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1364"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*> são fornecidos para dar suporte à associação de dados de estado com cada rota para que o aplicativo possa tomar decisões com base em qual rota teve uma correspondência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1364"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*> are provided to support associating state data with each route so that the app can make decisions based on which route matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1365">Esses valores são definidos pelo desenvolvedor e **não** afetam de forma alguma o comportamento do roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1365">These values are developer-defined and do **not** affect the behavior of routing in any way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1366">Além disso, os valores em stash em [RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) podem ser de qualquer tipo, ao contrário de [RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values), que devem ser conversíveis de/para cadeias de caracteres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1366">Additionally, values stashed in [RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) can be of any type, in contrast to [RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values), which must be convertible to and from strings.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1367">[RouteData.Routers](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers) é uma lista das rotas que participaram da correspondência bem-sucedida da solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1367">[RouteData.Routers](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers) is a list of the routes that took part in successfully matching the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1368">As rotas podem ser aninhadas uma dentro da outra.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1368">Routes can be nested inside of one another.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1369">A propriedade <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> reflete o caminho pela árvore lógica de rotas que resultou em uma correspondência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1369">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> property reflects the path through the logical tree of routes that resulted in a match.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1370">Em geral, o primeiro item em <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> é a coleção de rotas e deve ser usado para a geração de URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1370">Generally, the first item in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> is the route collection and should be used for URL generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1371">O último item em <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> é o manipulador de rotas que teve uma correspondência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1371">The last item in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> is the route handler that matched.</span></span>

<a name="lg"></a>

### <a name="url-generation"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-1372">Geração de URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1372">URL generation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1373">Geração de URL é o processo pelo qual o roteamento pode criar um caminho de URL de acordo com um conjunto de valores de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1373">URL generation is the process by which routing can create a URL path based on a set of route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1374">Isso permite uma separação lógica entre os manipuladores de rotas e as URLs que os acessam.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1374">This allows for a logical separation between route handlers and the URLs that access them.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1375">A geração de URL segue um processo iterativo semelhante, mas começa com o código da estrutura ou do usuário chamando o método <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> da coleção de rotas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1375">URL generation follows a similar iterative process, but it starts with user or framework code calling into the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> method of the route collection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1376">Cada *rota* tem seu método <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> chamado em sequência, até que um <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData> não nulo seja retornado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1376">Each *route* has its <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> method called in sequence until a non-null <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData> is returned.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1377">As entradas primárias para <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> são:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1377">The primary inputs to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> are:</span></span>

* [<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1378">VirtualPathContext.HttpContext</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1378">VirtualPathContext.HttpContext</span></span>](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.HttpContext)
* [<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1379">VirtualPathContext.Values</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1379">VirtualPathContext.Values</span></span>](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.Values)
* [<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1380">VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1380">VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues</span></span>](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues)

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1381">As rotas usam principalmente os valores de rota fornecidos por <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.Values> e <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues> para decidir se é possível gerar uma URL e quais valores serão incluídos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1381">Routes primarily use the route values provided by <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.Values> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues> to decide whether it's possible to generate a URL and what values to include.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1382">Os <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues> são o conjunto de valores de rota produzidos pela correspondência da solicitação atual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1382">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues> are the set of route values that were produced from matching the current request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1383">Por outro lado, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.Values> são os valores de rota que especificam como gerar a URL desejada para a operação atual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1383">In contrast, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.Values> are the route values that specify how to generate the desired URL for the current operation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1384">O <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.HttpContext> é fornecido para o caso de uma rota precisar obter serviços ou dados adicionais associados ao contexto atual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1384">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.HttpContext> is provided in case a route should obtain services or additional data associated with the current context.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1385">Considere [VirtualPathContext.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.Values*) como um conjunto de substituições de [VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues*).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1385">Think of [VirtualPathContext.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.Values*) as a set of overrides for the [VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues*).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1386">A geração de URL tenta reutilizar os valores de rota da solicitação atual para gerar URLs para links usando a mesma rota ou os mesmos valores de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1386">URL generation attempts to reuse route values from the current request to generate URLs for links using the same route or route values.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1387">A saída de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> é um <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1387">The output of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> is a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1388"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData> é um paralelo de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1388"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData> is a parallel of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1389"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData> contém o <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> da URL de saída e algumas propriedades adicionais que devem ser definidas pela rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1389"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData> contains the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> for the output URL and some additional properties that should be set by the route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1390">A propriedade [VirtualPathData.VirtualPath](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath*) contém o *caminho virtual* produzido pela rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1390">The [VirtualPathData.VirtualPath](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath*) property contains the *virtual path* produced by the route.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1391">Dependendo das suas necessidades, talvez você precise processar ainda mais o caminho.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1391">Depending on your needs, you may need to process the path further.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1392">Se você desejar renderizar a URL gerada em HTML, preceda o caminho base do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1392">If you want to render the generated URL in HTML, prepend the base path of the app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1393">O [VirtualPathData.Router](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.Router*) é uma referência à rota que gerou a URL com êxito.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1393">The [VirtualPathData.Router](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.Router*) is a reference to the route that successfully generated the URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1394">As propriedades de [VirtualPathData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.DataTokens*) são um dicionário de dados adicionais relacionados à rota que gerou a URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1394">The [VirtualPathData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.DataTokens*) properties is a dictionary of additional data related to the route that generated the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1395">Isso é o paralelo de [RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1395">This is the parallel of [RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*).</span></span>

### <a name="create-routes"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-1396">Criar rotas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1396">Create routes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1397">O roteamento fornece a classe <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> como a implementação padrão de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1397">Routing provides the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class as the standard implementation of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1398"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> usa a sintaxe de *modelo de rota* para definir padrões que corresponderão ao caminho da URL quando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> for chamado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1398"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> uses the *route template* syntax to define patterns to match against the URL path when <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> is called.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1399"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> usa o mesmo modelo de rota para gerar uma URL quando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> é chamado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1399"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> uses the same route template to generate a URL when <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> is called.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1400">A maioria dos aplicativos cria rotas chamando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> ou um dos métodos de extensão semelhantes definidos em <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1400">Most apps create routes by calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> or one of the similar extension methods defined on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1401">Qualquer um dos métodos de extensão de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> cria uma instância de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> e a adicionam à coleção de rotas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1401">Any of the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> extension methods create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> and add it to the route collection.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1402"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> não aceita um parâmetro de manipulador de rotas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1402"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> doesn't accept a route handler parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1403"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> apenas adiciona rotas que são manipuladas pelo <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1403"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> only adds routes that are handled by the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1404">O manipulador padrão é um `IRouter`, e o manipulador não pode manipular a solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1404">The default handler is an `IRouter`, and the handler might not handle the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1405">Por exemplo, o ASP.NET Core MVC normalmente é configurado como um manipulador padrão que só manipula as solicitações que correspondem a um controlador e a uma ação disponíveis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1405">For example, ASP.NET Core MVC is typically configured as a default handler that only handles requests that match an available controller and action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1406">Para saber mais sobre o roteamento no MVC, confira <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1406">To learn more about routing in MVC, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1407">O exemplo de código a seguir é um exemplo de uma chamada <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> usada por uma definição de rota típica do ASP.NET Core MVC:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1407">The following code example is an example of a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> call used by a typical ASP.NET Core MVC route definition:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1408">Esse modelo corresponde a um caminho de URL e extrai os valores de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1408">This template matches a URL path and extracts the route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1409">Por exemplo, o caminho `/Products/Details/17` gera os seguintes valores de rota: `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 17 }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1409">For example, the path `/Products/Details/17` generates the following route values: `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 17 }`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1410">Os valores de rota são determinados pela divisão do caminho da URL em segmentos e pela correspondência de cada segmento com o nome do *parâmetro de rota* no modelo de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1410">Route values are determined by splitting the URL path into segments and matching each segment with the *route parameter* name in the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1411">Os parâmetros de rota são nomeados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1411">Route parameters are named.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1412">Os parâmetros são definidos com a colocação do nome do parâmetro em chaves `{ ... }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1412">The parameters defined by enclosing the parameter name in braces `{ ... }`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1413">O modelo anterior também pode corresponder ao caminho da URL `/` e produzir os valores `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1413">The preceding template could also match the URL path `/` and produce the values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1414">Isso ocorre porque os parâmetros de rota `{controller}` e `{action}` têm valores padrão e o parâmetro de rota `id` é opcional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1414">This occurs because the `{controller}` and `{action}` route parameters have default values and the `id` route parameter is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1415">Um sinal de igual (`=`) seguido de um valor após o nome do parâmetro de rota define um valor padrão para o parâmetro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1415">An equals sign (`=`) followed by a value after the route parameter name defines a default value for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1416">Um ponto de interrogação (`?`) após o nome do parâmetro de rota define o parâmetro como opcional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1416">A question mark (`?`) after the route parameter name defines an optional parameter.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1417">Os parâmetros de rota com um valor padrão *sempre* produzem um valor de rota quando a rota corresponde.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1417">Route parameters with a default value *always* produce a route value when the route matches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1418">Os parâmetros opcionais não produzem um valor de rota se não houver um segmento de caminho de URL correspondente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1418">Optional parameters don't produce a route value if there is no corresponding URL path segment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1419">Confira a seção [Referência de modelo de rota](#route-template-reference) para obter uma descrição completa dos recursos e da sintaxe de modelo de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1419">See the [Route template reference](#route-template-reference) section for a thorough description of route template scenarios and syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1420">No seguinte exemplo, a definição do parâmetro de rota `{id:int}` define uma [restrição de rota](#route-constraint-reference) para o parâmetro de rota `id`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1420">In the following example, the route parameter definition `{id:int}` defines a [route constraint](#route-constraint-reference) for the `id` route parameter:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id:int}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1421">Esse modelo corresponde a um caminho de URL, como `/Products/Details/17`, mas não como `/Products/Details/Apples`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1421">This template matches a URL path like `/Products/Details/17` but not `/Products/Details/Apples`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1422">As restrições de rota implementam <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> e inspecionam valores de rota para verificá-los.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1422">Route constraints implement <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> and inspect route values to verify them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1423">Neste exemplo, o valor de rota `id` precisa ser conversível em um inteiro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1423">In this example, the route value `id` must be convertible to an integer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1424">Confira [route-constraint-reference](#route-constraint-reference) para obter uma explicação das restrições de rota fornecidas pela estrutura.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1424">See [route-constraint-reference](#route-constraint-reference) for an explanation of route constraints provided by the framework.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1425">Sobrecargas adicionais de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> aceitam valores para `constraints`, `dataTokens` e `defaults`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1425">Additional overloads of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> accept values for `constraints`, `dataTokens`, and `defaults`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1426">O uso típico desses parâmetros é passar um objeto de tipo anônimo, no qual os nomes da propriedade do tipo anônimo correspondem aos nomes do parâmetro de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1426">The typical usage of these parameters is to pass an anonymously typed object, where the property names of the anonymous type match route parameter names.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1427">Os seguintes exemplos de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> criam rotas equivalentes:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1427">The following <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> examples create equivalent routes:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default_route",
    template: "{controller}/{action}/{id?}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Home", action = "Index" });

routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default_route",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1428">A sintaxe embutida para a definição de restrições e padrões pode ser interessante para rotas simples.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1428">The inline syntax for defining constraints and defaults can be convenient for simple routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1429">No entanto, há cenários, como tokens de dados, que não dão suporte à sintaxe embutida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1429">However, there are scenarios, such as data tokens, that aren't supported by inline syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1430">O seguinte exemplo demonstra mais alguns cenários:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1430">The following example demonstrates a few additional scenarios:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "blog",
    template: "Blog/{*article}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadArticle" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1431">O modelo anterior corresponde a um caminho de URL, como `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction`, e extrai os valores `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1431">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction` and extracts the values `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1432">Os valores de rota padrão para `controller` e `action` são produzidos pela rota, mesmo que não haja nenhum parâmetro de rota correspondente no modelo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1432">The default route values for `controller` and `action` are produced by the route even though there are no corresponding route parameters in the template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1433">Os valores padrão podem ser especificados no modelo de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1433">Default values can be specified in the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1434">O parâmetro de rota `article` é definido como um *catch-all* pela aparência de um asterisco (`*`) antes do nome do parâmetro de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1434">The `article` route parameter is defined as a *catch-all* by the appearance of an asterisk (`*`) before the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1435">Os parâmetros de rota catch-all capturam o restante do caminho de URL e também podem corresponder à cadeia de caracteres vazia.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1435">Catch-all route parameters capture the remainder of the URL path and can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1436">O seguinte exemplo adiciona restrições de rota e tokens de dados:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1436">The following example adds route constraints and data tokens:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "us_english_products",
    template: "en-US/Products/{id}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Products", action = "Details" },
    constraints: new { id = new IntRouteConstraint() },
    dataTokens: new { locale = "en-US" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1437">O modelo anterior corresponde a um caminho de URL como `/en-US/Products/5` e extrai os valores de `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` e os tokens de dados `{ locale = en-US }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1437">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/en-US/Products/5` and extracts the values `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` and the data tokens `{ locale = en-US }`.</span></span>

![Tokens locais do Windows](routing/_static/tokens.png)

### <a name="route-class-url-generation"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-1439">Geração de URL da classe de rota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1439">Route class URL generation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1440">A classe <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> também pode executar a geração de URL pela combinação de um conjunto de valores de rota com seu modelo de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1440">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class can also perform URL generation by combining a set of route values with its route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1441">Logicamente, este é o processo inverso de correspondência do caminho de URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1441">This is logically the reverse process of matching the URL path.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1442">Para entender melhor a geração de URL, imagine qual URL você deseja gerar e, em seguida, pense em como um modelo de rota corresponderia a essa URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1442">To better understand URL generation, imagine what URL you want to generate and then think about how a route template would match that URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1443">Quais valores serão produzidos?</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1443">What values would be produced?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1444">Este é o equivalente aproximado de como funciona a geração de URL na classe <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1444">This is the rough equivalent of how URL generation works in the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1445">O seguinte exemplo usa uma rota padrão geral do ASP.NET Core MVC:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1445">The following example uses a general ASP.NET Core MVC default route:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1446">Com os valores de rota `{ controller = Products, action = List }`, a URL `/Products/List` é gerada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1446">With the route values `{ controller = Products, action = List }`, the URL `/Products/List` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1447">Os valores de rota são substituídos pelos parâmetros de rota correspondentes para formar o caminho de URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1447">The route values are substituted for the corresponding route parameters to form the URL path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1448">Como `id` é um parâmetro de rota opcional, a URL é gerada com êxito sem um valor para `id`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1448">Since `id` is an optional route parameter, the URL is successfully generated without a value for `id`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1449">Com os valores de rota `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`, a URL `/` é gerada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1449">With the route values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`, the URL `/` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1450">Os valores de rota fornecidos correspondem aos valores padrão, sendo que os segmentos correspondentes aos valores padrão são omitidos com segurança.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1450">The provided route values match the default values, and the segments corresponding to the default values are safely omitted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1451">A viagem de ida e volta gerada pelas duas URLs com a definição de rota a seguir (`/Home/Index` e `/`) produz os mesmos valores de rota que foram usados para gerar a URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1451">Both URLs generated round-trip with the following route definition (`/Home/Index` and `/`) produce the same route values that were used to generate the URL.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1452">Um aplicativo que usa o ASP.NET Core MVC deve usar <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> para gerar URLs, em vez de chamar o roteamento diretamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1452">An app using ASP.NET Core MVC should use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> to generate URLs instead of calling into routing directly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1453">Para obter mais informações sobre a geração de URL, confira a seção [Referência de geração de URL](#url-generation-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1453">For more information on URL generation, see the [Url generation reference](#url-generation-reference) section.</span></span>

## <a name="use-routing-middleware"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-1454">Use middleware de roteamento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1454">Use routing middleware</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1455">Referencie o [metapacote Microsoft.AspNetCore.App](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app) no arquivo de projeto do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1455">Reference the [Microsoft.AspNetCore.App metapackage](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app) in the app's project file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1456">Adicione o roteamento ao contêiner de serviço em `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1456">Add routing to the service container in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_ConfigureServices&highlight=3)]

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1457">As rotas precisam ser configuradas no método `Startup.Configure`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1457">Routes must be configured in the `Startup.Configure` method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1458">O aplicativo de exemplo usa as seguintes APIs:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1458">The sample app uses the following APIs:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>
* <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1459"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>&ndash; Corresponde apenas às solicitações HTTP GET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1459"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> &ndash; Matches only HTTP GET requests.</span></span>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_RouteHandler)]

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1460">A tabela a seguir mostra as respostas com os URIs fornecidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1460">The following table shows the responses with the given URIs.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1461">URI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1461">URI</span></span>                    | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1462">Resposta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1462">Response</span></span>                                          |
| ---------------------- | ------------------------------------------------- |
| `/package/create/3`    | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1463">Olá!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1463">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1464">Valores de rota: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1464">Route values: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3`    | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1465">Olá!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1465">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1466">Valores de rota: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1466">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3/`   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1467">Olá!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1467">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1468">Valores de rota: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1468">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/`      | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1469">A solicitação é ignorada; sem correspondência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1469">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |
| `GET /hello/Joe`       | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1470">Olá, Joe!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1470">Hi, Joe!</span></span>                                          |
| `POST /hello/Joe`      | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1471">A solicitação é ignorada; corresponde apenas a HTTP GET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1471">The request falls through, matches HTTP GET only.</span></span> |
| `GET /hello/Joe/Smith` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1472">A solicitação é ignorada; sem correspondência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1472">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1473">Se você estiver configurando uma única rota, chame <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*> passando uma instância de `IRouter`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1473">If you're configuring a single route, call <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*> passing in an `IRouter` instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1474">Você não precisa usar <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1474">You won't need to use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1475">A estrutura fornece um conjunto de métodos de extensão para a criação de rotas (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1475">The framework provides a set of extension methods for creating routes (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>):</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareVerb*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1476">Alguns dos métodos listados, como <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, exigem um <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1476">Some of listed methods, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, require a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1477">O <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate> é usado como o *manipulador de rotas* quando a rota corresponde.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1477">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate> is used as the *route handler* when the route matches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1478">Outros métodos nesta família permitem configurar um pipeline de middleware a ser usado como o manipulador de rotas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1478">Other methods in this family allow configuring a middleware pipeline for use as the route handler.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1479">Se o método `Map*` não aceitar um manipulador, como <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>, ele usará o <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1479">If the `Map*` method doesn't accept a handler, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>, it uses the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1480">Os métodos `Map[Verb]` usam restrições para limitar a rota ao Verbo HTTP no nome do método.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1480">The `Map[Verb]` methods use constraints to limit the route to the HTTP Verb in the method name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1481">Por exemplo, veja <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> e <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1481">For example, see <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span></span>

## <a name="route-template-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-1482">Referência de modelo de rota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1482">Route template reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1483">Os tokens entre chaves (`{ ... }`) definem os *parâmetros de rota* que serão associados se a rota for correspondida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1483">Tokens within curly braces (`{ ... }`) define *route parameters* that are bound if the route is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1484">Você pode definir mais de um parâmetro de rota em um segmento de rota, mas eles precisam ser separados por um valor literal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1484">You can define more than one route parameter in a route segment, but they must be separated by a literal value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1485">Por exemplo, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` não é uma rota válida, já que não há nenhum valor literal entre `{controller}` e `{action}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1485">For example, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` isn't a valid route, since there's no literal value between `{controller}` and `{action}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1486">Esses parâmetros de rota precisam ter um nome e podem ter atributos adicionais especificados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1486">These route parameters must have a name and may have additional attributes specified.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1487">Um texto literal diferente dos parâmetros de rota (por exemplo, `{id}`) e do separador de caminho `/` precisa corresponder ao texto na URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1487">Literal text other than route parameters (for example, `{id}`) and the path separator `/` must match the text in the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1488">A correspondência de texto não diferencia maiúsculas de minúsculas e se baseia na representação decodificada do caminho de URLs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1488">Text matching is case-insensitive and based on the decoded representation of the URLs path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1489">Para encontrar a correspondência de um delimitador de parâmetro de rota literal (`{` ou `}`), faça o escape do delimitador repetindo o caractere (`{{` ou `}}`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1489">To match a literal route parameter delimiter (`{` or `}`), escape the delimiter by repeating the character (`{{` or `}}`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1490">Padrões de URL que tentam capturar um nome de arquivo com uma extensão de arquivo opcional apresentam considerações adicionais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1490">URL patterns that attempt to capture a file name with an optional file extension have additional considerations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1491">Por exemplo, considere o modelo `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1491">For example, consider the template `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1492">Quando existem valores para `filename` e `ext`, ambos os valores são populados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1492">When values for both `filename` and `ext` exist, both values are populated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1493">Se apenas existir um valor para `filename` na URL, a rota encontrará uma correspondência, pois o ponto à direita (`.`) é opcional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1493">If only a value for `filename` exists in the URL, the route matches because the trailing period (`.`) is  optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1494">As URLs a seguir correspondem a essa rota:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1494">The following URLs match this route:</span></span>

* `/files/myFile.txt`
* `/files/myFile`

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1495">Você pode usar o asterisco (`*`) como um prefixo para um parâmetro de rota a ser associado ao restante do URI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1495">You can use the asterisk (`*`) as a prefix to a route parameter to bind to the rest of the URI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1496">Isso é chamado de parâmetro *catch-all*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1496">This is called a *catch-all* parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1497">Por exemplo, `blog/{*slug}` corresponde a qualquer URI que começa com `/blog` e tem qualquer valor depois dele, que é atribuído ao valor de rota `slug`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1497">For example, `blog/{*slug}` matches any URI that starts with `/blog` and has any value following it, which is assigned to the `slug` route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1498">Os parâmetros catch-all também podem corresponder à cadeia de caracteres vazia.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1498">Catch-all parameters can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1499">O parâmetro catch-all faz o escape dos caracteres corretos quando a rota é usada para gerar uma URL, incluindo os caracteres separadores de caminho (`/`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1499">The catch-all parameter escapes the appropriate characters when the route is used to generate a URL, including path separator (`/`) characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1500">Por exemplo, a rota `foo/{*path}` com valores de rota `{ path = "my/path" }` gera `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1500">For example, the route `foo/{*path}` with route values `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1501">Observe o escape da barra invertida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1501">Note the escaped forward slash.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1502">Os parâmetros de rota podem ter *valores padrão*, designados pela especificação do valor padrão após o nome do parâmetro separado por um sinal de igual (`=`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1502">Route parameters may have *default values* designated by specifying the default value after the parameter name separated by an equals sign (`=`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1503">Por exemplo, `{controller=Home}` define `Home` como o valor padrão de `controller`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1503">For example, `{controller=Home}` defines `Home` as the default value for `controller`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1504">O valor padrão é usado se nenhum valor está presente na URL para o parâmetro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1504">The default value is used if no value is present in the URL for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1505">Os parâmetros de rota se tornam opcionais com o acréscimo de um ponto de interrogação (`?`) ao final do nome do parâmetro, como em `id?`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1505">Route parameters are made optional by appending a question mark (`?`) to the end of the parameter name, as in `id?`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1506">A diferença entre valores opcionais e parâmetros de rota padrão é que um parâmetro de rota com um valor padrão sempre produz um valor – um parâmetro opcional tem um valor somente quando um valor é fornecido pela URL de solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1506">The difference between optional values and default route parameters is that a route parameter with a default value always produces a value&mdash;an optional parameter has a value only when a value is provided by the request URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1507">Os parâmetros de rota podem ter restrições que precisam corresponder ao valor de rota associado da URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1507">Route parameters may have constraints that must match the route value bound from the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1508">A adição de dois-pontos (`:`) e do nome da restrição após o nome do parâmetro de rota especifica uma *restrição embutida* em um parâmetro de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1508">Adding a colon (`:`) and constraint name after the route parameter name specifies an *inline constraint* on a route parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1509">Se a restrição exigir argumentos, eles ficarão entre parênteses (`(...)`) após o nome da restrição.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1509">If the constraint requires arguments, they're enclosed in parentheses (`(...)`) after the constraint name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1510">Várias restrições embutidas podem ser especificadas por meio do acréscimo de outros dois-pontos (`:`) e do nome da restrição.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1510">Multiple inline constraints can be specified by appending another colon (`:`) and constraint name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1511">O nome da restrição e os argumentos são passados para o serviço <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> para criar uma instância de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> a ser usada no processamento de URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1511">The constraint name and arguments are passed to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> service to create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> to use in URL processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1512">Por exemplo, o modelo de rota `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` especifica uma restrição `minlength` com o argumento `10`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1512">For example, the route template `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifies a `minlength` constraint with the argument `10`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1513">Para obter mais informações sobre as restrições de rota e uma lista das restrições fornecidas pela estrutura, confira a seção [Referência de restrição de rota](#route-constraint-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1513">For more information on route constraints and a list of the constraints provided by the framework, see the [Route constraint reference](#route-constraint-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1514">A tabela a seguir demonstra modelos de rota de exemplo e seu comportamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1514">The following table demonstrates example route templates and their behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1515">Modelo de rota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1515">Route Template</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1516">URI de correspondência de exemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1516">Example Matching URI</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1517">O URI de solicitação&hellip;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1517">The request URI&hellip;</span></span>                                                    |
| ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `hello`                                  | `/hello`                | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1518">Somente corresponde ao caminho único `/hello`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1518">Only matches the single path `/hello`.</span></span>                                     |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1519">Faz a correspondência e define `Page` como `Home`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1519">Matches and sets `Page` to `Home`.</span></span>                                         |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/Contact`              | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1520">Faz a correspondência e define `Page` como `Contact`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1520">Matches and sets `Page` to `Contact`.</span></span>                                      |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/List`        | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1521">É mapeado para o controlador `Products` e a ação `List`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1521">Maps to the `Products` controller and `List` action.</span></span>                       |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/Details/123` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1522">É mapeado para o controlador `Products` e a ação `Details` (`id` definido como 123).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1522">Maps to the `Products` controller and  `Details` action (`id` set to 123).</span></span> |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1523">É mapeado para o controlador `Home` e o método `Index` (`id` é ignorado).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1523">Maps to the `Home` controller and `Index` method (`id` is ignored).</span></span>        |

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1524">Em geral, o uso de um modelo é a abordagem mais simples para o roteamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1524">Using a template is generally the simplest approach to routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1525">Restrições e padrões também podem ser especificados fora do modelo de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1525">Constraints and defaults can also be specified outside the route template.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1526">Habilite o [Log](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) para ver como as implementações de roteamento internas, como <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, correspondem às solicitações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1526">Enable [Logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) to see how the built-in routing implementations, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, match requests.</span></span>

## <a name="route-constraint-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-1527">Referência de restrição de rota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1527">Route constraint reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1528">As restrições de rota são executadas quando ocorre uma correspondência com a URL de entrada e é criado um token do caminho da URL em valores de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1528">Route constraints execute when a match has occurred to the incoming URL and the URL path is tokenized into route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1529">Em geral, as restrições da rota inspecionam o valor de rota associado por meio do modelo de rota e tomam uma decisão do tipo "sim/não" sobre se o valor é aceitável ou não.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1529">Route constraints generally inspect the route value associated via the route template and make a yes/no decision about whether or not the value is acceptable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1530">Algumas restrições da rota usam dados fora do valor de rota para considerar se a solicitação pode ser encaminhada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1530">Some route constraints use data outside the route value to consider whether the request can be routed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1531">Por exemplo, a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> pode aceitar ou rejeitar uma solicitação de acordo com o verbo HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1531">For example, the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> can accept or reject a request based on its HTTP verb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1532">As restrições são usadas em solicitações de roteamento e na geração de link.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1532">Constraints are used in routing requests and link generation.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1533">Não use restrições para a **validação de entrada**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1533">Don't use constraints for **input validation**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1534">Se as restrições forem usadas para a **validação de entrada**, uma entrada inválida resultará em uma resposta *404 – Não Encontrado*, em vez de *400 – Solicitação Inválida* com uma mensagem de erro apropriada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1534">If constraints are used for **input validation**, invalid input results in a *404 - Not Found* response instead of a *400 - Bad Request* with an appropriate error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1535">As restrições de rota são usadas para **desfazer a ambiguidade** entre rotas semelhantes, não para validar as entradas de uma rota específica.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1535">Route constraints are used to **disambiguate** similar routes, not to validate the inputs for a particular route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1536">A tabela a seguir demonstra restrições de rota de exemplo e seu comportamento esperado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1536">The following table demonstrates example route constraints and their expected behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1537">restrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1537">constraint</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1538">Exemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1538">Example</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1539">Correspondências de exemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1539">Example Matches</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1540">Observações</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1540">Notes</span></span> |
| ---------- | ------- | --------------- | ----- |
| `int` | `{id:int}` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1541">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1541">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1542">Corresponde a qualquer inteiro</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1542">Matches any integer</span></span> |
| `bool` | `{active:bool}` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1543">`true`, `FALSE`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1543">`true`, `FALSE`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1544">Corresponde a `true` ou `false` (não diferencia maiúsculas de minúsculas)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1544">Matches `true` or `false` (case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `datetime` | `{dob:datetime}` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1545">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1545">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1546">Corresponde a `DateTime` um valor válido na cultura invariante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1546">Matches a valid `DateTime` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1547">Veja o aviso anterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1547">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `decimal` | `{price:decimal}` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1548">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1548">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1549">Corresponde a `decimal` um valor válido na cultura invariante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1549">Matches a valid `decimal` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1550">Veja o aviso anterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1550">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `double` | `{weight:double}` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1551">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1551">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1552">Corresponde a `double` um valor válido na cultura invariante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1552">Matches a valid `double` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1553">Veja o aviso anterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1553">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `float` | `{weight:float}` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1554">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1554">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1555">Corresponde a `float` um valor válido na cultura invariante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1555">Matches a valid `float` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1556">Veja o aviso anterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1556">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `guid` | `{id:guid}` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1557">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1557">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1558">Corresponde a um valor `Guid` válido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1558">Matches a valid `Guid` value</span></span> |
| `long` | `{ticks:long}` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1559">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1559">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1560">Corresponde a um valor `long` válido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1560">Matches a valid `long` value</span></span> |
| `minlength(value)` | `{username:minlength(4)}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1561">A cadeia de caracteres deve ter, no mínimo, 4 caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1561">String must be at least 4 characters</span></span> |
| `maxlength(value)` | `{filename:maxlength(8)}` | `Richard` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1562">A cadeia de caracteres não pode ser maior que 8 caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1562">String must be no more than 8 characters</span></span> |
| `length(length)` | `{filename:length(12)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1563">A cadeia de caracteres deve ter exatamente 12 caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1563">String must be exactly 12 characters long</span></span> |
| `length(min,max)` | `{filename:length(8,16)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1564">A cadeia de caracteres deve ter, pelo menos, 8 e não mais de 16 caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1564">String must be at least 8 and no more than 16 characters long</span></span> |
| `min(value)` | `{age:min(18)}` | `19` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1565">O valor inteiro deve ser, pelo menos, 18</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1565">Integer value must be at least 18</span></span> |
| `max(value)` | `{age:max(120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1566">O valor inteiro não deve ser maior que 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1566">Integer value must be no more than 120</span></span> |
| `range(min,max)` | `{age:range(18,120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1567">O valor inteiro deve ser, pelo menos, 18, mas não maior que 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1567">Integer value must be at least 18 but no more than 120</span></span> |
| `alpha` | `{name:alpha}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1568">A cadeia de caracteres deve consistir em um ou mais caracteres alfabéticos (`a`-`z`, não diferencia maiúsculas de minúsculas)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1568">String must consist of one or more alphabetical characters (`a`-`z`, case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `regex(expression)` | `{ssn:regex(^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$)}` | `123-45-6789` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1569">A cadeia de caracteres deve corresponder à expressão regular (veja as dicas sobre como definir uma expressão regular)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1569">String must match the regular expression (see tips about defining a regular expression)</span></span> |
| `required` | `{name:required}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1570">Usado para impor que um valor não parâmetro está presente durante a geração de URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1570">Used to enforce that a non-parameter value is present during URL generation</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1571">Várias restrições delimitadas por vírgula podem ser aplicadas a um único parâmetro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1571">Multiple, colon-delimited constraints can be applied to a single parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1572">Por exemplo, a restrição a seguir restringe um parâmetro para um valor inteiro de 1 ou maior:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1572">For example, the following constraint restricts a parameter to an integer value of 1 or greater:</span></span>

```csharp
[Route("users/{id:int:min(1)}")]
public User GetUserById(int id) { }
```

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1573">As restrições de rota que verificam a URL e são convertidas em um tipo CLR (como `int` ou `DateTime`) sempre usam a cultura invariável.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1573">Route constraints that verify the URL and are converted to a CLR type (such as `int` or `DateTime`) always use the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1574">Essas restrições consideram que a URL não é localizável.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1574">These constraints assume that the URL is non-localizable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1575">As restrições de rota fornecidas pela estrutura não modificam os valores armazenados nos valores de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1575">The framework-provided route constraints don't modify the values stored in route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1576">Todos os valores de rota analisados com base na URL são armazenados como cadeias de caracteres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1576">All route values parsed from the URL are stored as strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1577">Por exemplo, a restrição `float` tenta converter o valor de rota em um float, mas o valor convertido é usado somente para verificar se ele pode ser convertido em um float.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1577">For example, the `float` constraint attempts to convert the route value to a float, but the converted value is used only to verify it can be converted to a float.</span></span>

## <a name="regular-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-1578">Expressões regulares</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1578">Regular expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1579">A estrutura do ASP.NET Core adiciona `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` ao construtor de expressão regular.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1579">The ASP.NET Core framework adds `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` to the regular expression constructor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1580">Confira <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> para obter uma descrição desses membros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1580">See <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> for a description of these members.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1581">As expressões regulares usam delimitadores e tokens semelhantes aos usados pelo Roteamento e pela linguagem C#.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1581">Regular expressions use delimiters and tokens similar to those used by Routing and the C# language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1582">Os tokens de expressão regular precisam ter escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1582">Regular expression tokens must be escaped.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1583">Para usar a expressão regular `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` no roteamento, a expressão precisa ter os caracteres `\` (barra invertida) fornecidos na cadeia de caracteres como caracteres `\\` (barra invertida dupla) no arquivo de origem C# para fazer o escape do caractere de escape da cadeia de caracteres `\` (a menos que estejam sendo usados [literais de cadeia de caracteres textuais](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1583">To use the regular expression `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` in routing, the expression must have the `\` (single backslash) characters provided in the string as `\\` (double backslash) characters in the C# source file in order to escape the `\` string escape character (unless using [verbatim string literals](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1584">Para fazer o escape dos caracteres de delimitador de parâmetro de roteamento (`{`, `}`, `[`, `]`), duplique os caracteres na expressão (`{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1584">To escape routing parameter delimiter characters (`{`, `}`, `[`, `]`), double the characters in the expression (`{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1585">A tabela a seguir mostra uma expressão regular e a versão com escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1585">The following table shows a regular expression and the escaped version.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1586">Expressão regular</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1586">Regular Expression</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1587">Expressão regular com escape</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1587">Escaped Regular Expression</span></span>     |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` | `^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$` |
| `^[a-z]{2}$`          | `^[[a-z]]{{2}}$`               |
