<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1588">As expressões regulares usadas no roteamento geralmente começam com o caractere de acento circunflexo (`^`) e correspondem à posição inicial da cadeia de caracteres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1588">Regular expressions used in routing often start with the caret (`^`) character and match starting position of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1589">As expressões geralmente terminam com o caractere de cifrão (`$`) e correspondem ao final da cadeia de caracteres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1589">The expressions often end with the dollar sign (`$`) character and match end of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1590">Os caracteres `^` e `$` garantem que a expressão regular corresponde a todo o valor do parâmetro de rota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1590">The `^` and `$` characters ensure that the regular expression match the entire route parameter value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1591">Sem os caracteres `^` e `$`, a expressão regular corresponde a qualquer subcadeia de caracteres na cadeia de caracteres, o que geralmente não é o desejado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1591">Without the `^` and `$` characters, the regular expression match any substring within the string, which is often undesirable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1592">A tabela a seguir fornece exemplos e explica por que eles encontram ou não uma correspondência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1592">The following table provides examples and explains why they match or fail to match.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1593">Expression</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1593">Expression</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1594">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1594">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1595">Corresponder a</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1595">Match</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1596">Comentário</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1596">Comment</span></span>               |
| ------------ | --------- | :---: |  -------------------- |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1597">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1597">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1598">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1598">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1599">A subcadeia de caracteres corresponde</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1599">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1600">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1600">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1601">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1601">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1602">A subcadeia de caracteres corresponde</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1602">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1603">mz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1603">mz</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1604">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1604">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1605">Corresponde à expressão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1605">Matches expression</span></span>    |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1606">MZ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1606">MZ</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1607">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1607">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1608">Não diferencia maiúsculas de minúsculas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1608">Not case sensitive</span></span>    |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1609">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1609">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1610">Não</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1610">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1611">Confira `^` e `$` acima</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1611">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1612">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1612">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1613">Não</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1613">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1614">Confira `^` e `$` acima</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1614">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1615">Para saber mais sobre a sintaxe de expressões regulares, confira [Expressões regulares do .NET Framework](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1615">For more information on regular expression syntax, see [.NET Framework Regular Expressions](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1616">Para restringir um parâmetro a um conjunto conhecido de valores possíveis, use uma expressão regular.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1616">To constrain a parameter to a known set of possible values, use a regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1617">Por exemplo, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` apenas corresponde o valor da rota `action` a `list`, `get` ou `create`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1617">For example, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` only matches the `action` route value to `list`, `get`, or `create`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1618">Se passada para o dicionário de restrições, a cadeia de caracteres `^(list|get|create)$` é equivalente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1618">If passed into the constraints dictionary, the string `^(list|get|create)$` is equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1619">As restrições passadas para o dicionário de restrições (não embutidas em um modelo) que não correspondem a uma das restrições conhecidas também são tratadas como expressões regulares.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1619">Constraints that are passed in the constraints dictionary (not inline within a template) that don't match one of the known constraints are also treated as regular expressions.</span></span>

## <a name="custom-route-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-1620">Restrições de rota personalizadas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1620">Custom Route Constraints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1621">Além das restrições de rota internas, é possível criar restrições de rota personalizadas com a implementação da interface do <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1621">In addition to the built-in route constraints, custom route constraints can be created by implementing the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1622">A interface do <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> contém um único método, `Match`, que retorna `true` quando a restrição é satisfeita. Caso contrário, retorna `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1622">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface contains a single method, `Match`, which returns `true` if the constraint is satisfied and `false` otherwise.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1623">Para usar uma <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> personalizada, o tipo de restrição de rota deve ser registrado com o <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> do aplicativo, no contêiner de serviço do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1623">To use a custom <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>, the route constraint type must be registered with the app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in the app's service container.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1624">O <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> é um dicionário que mapeia as chaves de restrição de rota para implementações de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> que validam essas restrições.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1624">A <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> is a dictionary that maps route constraint keys to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> implementations that validate those constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1625">É possível atualizar o <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> do aplicativo no `Startup.ConfigureServices` como parte de uma chamada [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) ou configurando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> diretamente com `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1625">An app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> can be updated in `Startup.ConfigureServices` either as part of a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) call or by configuring <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directly with `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1626">Por exemplo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1626">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    options.ConstraintMap.Add("customName", typeof(MyCustomConstraint));
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1627">a restrição pode então ser aplicada às rotas da maneira usual, usando o nome especificado ao registrar o tipo de restrição.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1627">The constraint can then be applied to routes in the usual manner, using the name specified when registering the constraint type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1628">Por exemplo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1628">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
[HttpGet("{id:customName}")]
public ActionResult<string> Get(string id)
```

## <a name="url-generation-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-1629">Referência de geração de URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1629">URL generation reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1630">O exemplo a seguir mostra como gerar um link para uma rota com base em um dicionário de valores de rota e em um <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1630">The following example shows how to generate a link to a route given a dictionary of route values and a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_Dictionary)]

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1631">O <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> gerado no final do exemplo anterior é `/package/create/123`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1631">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generated at the end of the preceding sample is `/package/create/123`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1632">O dicionário fornece os valores de rota `operation` e `id` do modelo "Rastrear rota do pacote", `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1632">The dictionary supplies the `operation` and `id` route values of the "Track Package Route" template, `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1633">Para obter detalhes, consulte o código de exemplo na seção [Usar o middleware de roteamento](#use-routing-middleware) ou no [aplicativo de exemplo](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1633">For details, see the sample code in the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section or the [sample app](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1634">O segundo parâmetro para o construtor <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> é uma coleção de *valores de ambiente*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1634">The second parameter to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> constructor is a collection of *ambient values*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1635">Os valores de ambiente são convenientes de serem usados porque limitam o número de valores que um desenvolvedor precisa especificar em um contexto de solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1635">Ambient values are convenient to use because they limit the number of values a developer must specify within a request context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1636">Os valores de rota atuais da solicitação atual são considerados valores de ambiente para a geração de link.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1636">The current route values of the current request are considered ambient values for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1637">Na ação `About` de um aplicativo ASP.NET Core MVC do `HomeController`, não é necessário especificar o valor de rota do controlador a ser vinculado à ação `Index` – o valor de ambiente `Home` é usado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1637">In an ASP.NET Core MVC app's `About` action of the `HomeController`, you don't need to specify the controller route value to link to the `Index` action&mdash;the ambient value of `Home` is used.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1638">Os valores de ambiente que não correspondem a um parâmetro são ignorados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1638">Ambient values that don't match a parameter are ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1639">Os valores de ambiente também são ignorados quando um valor fornecido explicitamente substitui o valor de ambiente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1639">Ambient values are also ignored when an explicitly provided value overrides the ambient value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1640">A correspondência ocorre da esquerda para a direita na URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1640">Matching occurs from left to right in the URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1641">Valores fornecidos explicitamente, mas que não correspondem a um segmento da rota, são adicionados à cadeia de consulta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1641">Values explicitly provided but that don't match a segment of the route are added to the query string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1642">A tabela a seguir mostra o resultado do uso do modelo de rota `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1642">The following table shows the result when using the route template `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1643">Valores de ambiente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1643">Ambient Values</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1644">Valores explícitos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1644">Explicit Values</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1645">Result</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1645">Result</span></span>                  |
| ---------------------------------- | -------------------------------------- | ----------------------- |
| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1646">controlador = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1646">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1647">ação = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1647">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1648">controlador = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1648">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1649">controlador = "Order", ação = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1649">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span></span> | `/Order/About`          |
| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1650">controlador = "Home", cor = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1650">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1651">ação = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1651">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1652">controlador = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1652">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1653">ação = "About", cor = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1653">action = "About", color = "Red"</span></span>        | `/Home/About?color=Red` |

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1654">Se uma rota tem um valor padrão que não corresponde a um parâmetro e esse valor é fornecido de forma explícita, ele precisa corresponder ao valor padrão:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1654">If a route has a default value that doesn't correspond to a parameter and that value is explicitly provided, it must match the default value:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute("blog_route", "blog/{*slug}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadPost" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1655">A geração de link somente gera um link para essa rota quando os valores correspondentes de `controller` e `action` são fornecidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1655">Link generation only generates a link for this route when the matching values for `controller` and `action` are provided.</span></span>

## <a name="complex-segments"></a><span data-ttu-id="444c2-1656">Segmentos complexos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1656">Complex segments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="444c2-1657">Segmentos complexos (por exemplo, `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) são processados por meio da combinação de literais da direita para a esquerda, de uma maneira diferente de Greedy.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1657">Complex segments (for example `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) are processed by matching up literals from right to left in a non-greedy way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1658">Confira [este código](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) para ver uma explicação detalhada de como os segmentos complexos são combinados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1658">See [this code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) for a detailed explanation of how complex segments are matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="444c2-1659">O [exemplo de código](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) não é usado pelo ASP.NET Core, mas fornece uma explicação adequada sobre segmentos complexos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="444c2-1659">The [code sample](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) is not used by ASP.NET Core, but it provides a good explanation of complex segments.</span></span>

::: moniker-end
